1b1(rgyud): rgya gar skad du// ar+ya a mo g+ha pa sha ka la pa rA tsa bod skad du/ 'phags pa don yod pa'i zhags pa'i
1b2(rgyud): cho ga zhing mo'i rgyal po// bam po dang bre// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub seMs/ 
1b3(rgyud): dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'dra stegs pa spyan ras gzugs kyi dbang phyug 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa/ 
1b4(rgyud): dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das bo po ta ldan/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi pho brang shing rdzas la dang / tam la dang / tsam
1b5(rgyud): pa ka dang / mya ngan tshang dang / a ti mug ta ka sna tshogs mang pos legs par brgyan pa na/ dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po brgya stong dang / 
1b6(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sa ya bye ma brgya stong phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ gnas rtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha'i bu
2a1(rgyud): brgya stong du mas yongasu bskor cing mdun gyis bltas pa na/ dbang phyug dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / tshangs pa dang / lha'i bu rnams kyi dbang / 
2a2(rgyud): mdzad nas/ chos ston pa mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug stan las langs te/ 
2a3(rgyud): bla gos 'phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la
2a4(rgyud): ba de logs su 'dzum pa'i gzhin gyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol te// bcom ldan 'ad gang 'di don yod pa'i rgyal po'i snying po
2a5(rgyud): zhes bgyi ba mchis te/ bdag gis bskal pa dgu bcu rtsa gcig gi sngon logs su/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par blta bar/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jug
2a6(rgyud): rten dbang phyug rgyal po las mnos nas/ 'di ltar bdag gis dbang phyug dang / dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa lha'i bu rnams dang / gnas kyang ma'i
2a7(rgyud): lha'i bu brgya stong phrag mang po bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'dzin du brtsal nas bdag gi rmongs pa ma mchis pa'i ye shes bkod pa la sros
2b1(rgyud): nga'i ting nge 'dzin na rgyu stong phrag mang po thob par bgyi lagaso// bcom ldan 'das 'di ltar yangs phyogs gang du snying po 'di spyod pa'i sa phyogs de dang / dbang phyu/ 
2b2(rgyud): dab dbang phyug chen po lasogs pa lha'i bu khri'is stong bsrung ba dang / snga ba'i srang du gnas par rig por 'gyi lags so// bcom ldan 'das gang mngon yod pa phun/ 
2b3(rgyud): sum 'tshogs pa'i snying po 'di spyod pa phyogs de mched rten du bkur bar 'gyur lags so// bcom ldan 'das pang sems can de dag ni sangs rgyas bye ba khrag
2b4(rgyud): khrig stong phrag brgya la dge ba'i rtsa ba ba skyed par 'gyur lagaso// gang zhig don yod pa'i zhags pa'i sna po 'di nyan par bgyid na/ bcom ldan 'das
2b5(rgyud): sdig pa spyod pa'am/ sdig pa'i chos kun du spyod pa'am/ 'phags pa la bskur pa 'debs pa'am/ dam pa'i chos spong ba 'am/ mnar med par gzhal ba'am/ sangs
2b6(rgyud): dang byang chub sems dpa'/ nyan thos dang sangs rgyas thams cad spong ba de 'gyod par 'gyur zhing / ma 'ongs pa na sdom pa thob par 'gyur lags so// bcom ldan
2b7(rgyud): 'das re shig de nyid kyis zhag gcig bsrung ba bgyis te/ bzlas parjod pa gyis na/ tshe 'di nyid la las de rnams dge ba dang / gdug pa dang gsal bar 'gyur ro/ 
3a1(rgyud): rims rten gcig pa ma/ nyin gnyis pa'am/ nyin gsum pa 'am/ zhin bzhi pa'am/ de bzhin du rims nyin bdun pa'am/ miganang ngam/ rna ba'i nad dang
3a2(rgyud): sgra'i nad dom/ so dang mchu'i nad ma lce dang rkan gyi nang ngam/ snying gi nang ngam/ lto ba'i nad dam/ ro rgyab dang rkyad pa'i nad dam/ yan lag dang nying lag gi nad ngam/ gzhang
3a3(rgyud): 'gram 'am pho ba'i nad ngam/ tshad pa'am lag pa'am rkang pa'i nad dam/ klang pa'i nad dam sha kra chen po'am/ sha za'i nAd dam/ mdze'am rkang shu'am/ 
3a4(rgyud): 'brum bu phra mo 'am/ ldog pa 'am/ mtshan ma brdol pa'am/ 'bram bu'am/ rjed byed dam/ byang sde mas so/ gzhan gyis bsod cing / mching ba 'am brde/ 
3a5(rgyud): pa 'am/ bden pa ma lags pa'i bskur pa 'debs pa'am/ bcom ldan 'das mdor na lus kyi gdung ba'am/ sems kyi gdung ba'am/ rmi lam ngan pa'i las de yongs
3a6(rgyud): gdugs par 'gyur na/ sems can dag lhag par dad pa rnams kyis yongasu bya bar 'gyur ba lta smos kyang ci 'tshal/ bcom ldan 'das 'khor bzhi'am/ rigs bzhi las
3a7(rgyud): gang dag sgyu dang g.yos/ bdag gi don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po nyan par bgyid/ 'dzin par bgyid/ 'chang bar bgyid klog par 'drir 'jug par bgyid/ kun chub
3b1(rgyud): par bgyid/ sems can gzhan la yang sgrog par bgyid cing / tha na dud 'gro'i skye gnas su rtogs pa rnaMs kyi rna khung du btang de bzlas brjod bgyid la tshig 'di rnas sems
3b2(rgyud): par bgyid cing te/ skur pa ma mchis pa dang / gzugs ma mchis pa dang / rnam par mi rtog pa dang / kun du 'byung ba ma mchis pa dang / ring du 'gro ba ma mchis pa dang / bgyid
3b3(rgyud): pa ma mchis pa dang / gos pa ma mchis pa dang / sems mnyam pa nyid dang bral ba dang / phung po lnga dang bral ba ste/ rnal 'byor 'dis sangs rgyas rjes su dran
3b4(rgyud): par sgom par bgyid na/ de lta phyogs bcu nas sangs rgyas stong zhal ston par 'gyur zhing / nongs pa 'chags pa 'chags par 'gyur ba
3b5(rgyud): rgyas pa la sogs pa sbyar ro// klog bam du bgyis te khyim na 'chang bar bgyid dam/ rje dpon gyis bsgrag/ pas sam/ gzhan gyi ngor ram/ rang gzhan/ 
3b6(rgyud): gang tsam gyis rgyus zhan par bgyid na/ bcom ldan 'das mkhas pas/ 'phags pa sbyin ras gzigs dbang phyug gi 'brus de dag gi rma khung du sgra
3b7(rgyud): spags pa 'tshal bar bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das dper na skyes pa 'ga' zhig tsam ngom nam/ ga pur ram bla rtsi zhig la 'khros pas yongs su
4a1(rgyud): srad / rol btags nas/ bdag nyid la byugs nas/ tsan ngan nam ga pur+ya ram/ b+hU ci de 'di snyam du bdag la 'khros sam/ yongs su snga
4a2(rgyud): pas dI snum par mi bgyi'o// mi sems kyi gzhan du na de nyid la dri dga' bar 'gyid lags so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin du bdag gi don yod pa'i zhags
4a3(rgyud): ba'i snying po 'di yang gang su rung bas gzhang rgad dam/ tsam gyi zhes bya ba rgyas par sbyar ro// bcom ldan 'das g.yo sgyus mchod par bgyid na yang de nyid
4a4(rgyud): sems can du dA mu rgod dag gi dgeba'i rgyur 'gyur lags so// gang dang gang du skye bar 'gyur ba/ tshul khrims dang ting 'dzin dang shes ra ba dang / 
4a5(rgyud): bsod nams kyi dri dang bral bar mi 'gyur te/ tshul khrims kyi dri drag dang bar bgyid pa lags so// bcom ldan 'a ngas gang yang rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs
4a6(rgyud): kyi bu mo'am/ dge slong pa'am dge slong ma 'am/ dge snyen pa'am dge snyen ma'am/ de las gzhan pa'i sems can su yang rung bas/ don yod pa'i zhag
4a7(rgyud): po'i snying po'i ched du yang gyi ngo'i tshes brgyad la brgyad bsrung ba bgyis / gzhan mi sba bar ngan yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po lan bdun bzlas brjod pakyis
4b1(rgyud): nA bcom ldan 'das de tshes 'di nyid la phan yon nyi shu rtsa gcig thob par 'gyur te/ nyi shu rtsa gcig gang zhes na/ 'di lta ste/ de'i lus la nad rnams 'byung ba
4b2(rgyud): mi 'gyur ro// de'i lus la las kyi dbang gis nad rnams byung na yang myur du zhi bar 'gyur zhing / lus mdangs dang ldan pa dang yid du 'ong bar 'gyur ro// skye bo mang po'i snying / 
4b3(rgyud): du sdug pa dang dbang po spos par 'gyuraro// de'i don rnams 'grub par 'gyur ro// de'i don grub pa yang chom rkun gyis 'phrog par mi 'gyur ro// zhugs kyis ma'i tshig
4b4(rgyud): chab kyis me 'tshal/ rgyal po'i mthus 'phyogs pa'i rngo mi thog par 'gyuraro// de'i las kyi mthu' rnams rgyas par 'gyur te/ ser bas ma
4b5(rgyud): lag so// chab kyi 'jigs pa dang / rlung dang me'i 'jigs pa 'am lags so// don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying pa thal ba dang tshul ldan bdun bzlas
4b6(rgyud): brjod bgyis bgyi nas/ zhing gi phyogs 'tshams dang steng 'og tu 'chis pa bgyis na/ gnod pa thas cad nye bar zhi bar 'gyur ro// gzi brjid dang mdangs lan
4b7(rgyud): 'phrog par rdo rngo mi thog zhing / sems can thams cad kyi snying du sdug pa dang yid 'thad par 'gyu ro// de la dgra'i 'jigs pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// dgra re'i zeng
4b8(rgyud): la 'jigs pa byung na myur du zhi bar 'gyur ro// de la mi ma lag pa'i 'jigs pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur te/ byad kyi 'jigs pa ma lags/ mkha' 'gro ma yis 'jigs
5a1(rgyud): pa ma lags te/ de la nyid mongs pa dang / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa drag po 'byung bar mi 'gyu ro// me dang mtshon gyis 'gum par mi 'gyuraro// de la yang lha rnaMs kyis rtag tu
5a2(rgyud): rgyun mi chad par bsrung ba dang skyob pa dang / sbed pa'i phyir gnas par mi 'gyur ro// gang dang gang du skye bar 'gyur bar byas pa dang / snying rje dang dga' ba dang / btang snyoms dang bral ba
5a3(rgyud): mi 'gyur te/ de phan yon nyi shu rtsa gci gra po 'di dag thob par 'gyur lag so// gzhan yang chos brgyad thob par 'gyur te/ brgyad gang zhe na/ 'gum pa'i dus su 'phags pa
5a4(rgyud): spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dge slong gi gzugasu mngon sum du zhal ston par 'gyuraro// bde bar 'chi ba'i dus byed/ par 'gyu ro// lta ba 'khrul par mi 'gyuraro// lag
5a5(rgyud): pa mi g.yob pa dang / rkang pa mi g.yob pa dang / gshang lha ma mchis pa dang // dri'i steng du 'chi ba'i dus byed par 'gyuraro// dran pa shin du nye bar gnas par 'gyur// kha sbub tu 'chi ba dus
5a6(rgyud): byed par mi 'gyuraro// 'gum pa'i dus na yang skabs pa mi bas par 'gyuraro// de yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing gang bu smon pa der skye bar 'gyur zhing / dge pa'i gshegs gnyen dang yang bral ba
5a7(rgyud): mi 'phrum nyon gcig bzhin tu bzlas brjod pagyi'o// chang dang shangs su dong dpa geng tung nga / sogs dang/ 'dres pa dag phrag sa dang / khyad par bzud na gnyer ba spang bar bya'o/ 
5b1(rgyud): don yod pa'i zhags pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di yang sems can rnams la mthu mchis pa dang / mthu mchis par 'tshal bar bgyid na bsgrag par bgyi'o// slob dpon gyi dpe khyud du
5b2(rgyud): mi bgyi'o// 'di ltar dri ma dang bral zhing 'phra dog dang ser sna spangs pa ni byang chub seMs rba rnaMs lags te/ sems kyi don pa'i slad du/ sangs rgyas byang chub thob par 'gyur bas/ byang chub seMs
5b3(rgyud): rba rnaMs kyi chog kyi nang du rtog so// byang chub ces gyi ba ni shes rab lag/ sems dpa' zhes bgyi ba thabs lags te/ chos 'di gnyis seMs can rnams kyi don dgyi ba'i slad du khyo nas thob pa lags
5b4(rgyud): gal te bco ldan 'das bdag la rje su gnad ra na/ ci ltar bdag gi snying po 'di de bzhin gsheg pa'i spyan sngar 'khor bzhi po rnaMs dang / gzhan yang sdig spyod pa rnaMs kyi don dang / sman pa dang bad/ 
5b5(rgyud): ba'i slad du bsgrags par bgyid do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub ses dpa' 'phags pa spyan ras gzig dang bang phyug la 'di skad ces bka' bstsal to// ses
5b6(rgyud): can dag pa de'i dus la bab par shes na/ khyod smros shig de bzhin gsheg pa rje su yid rang bar mdzad zin te/ phyi ma'i tshe phye ma'i dus na/ byang chub sems dpa' theg pa can rnas
5b7(rgyud): la pa'i bya ba byed par 'gyuraro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug mig mi btsum par/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
5b8(rgyud): ldan 'das byang chub seMsarba kyi thas cad kyis phyag bgyis pa/ rnaM bar grol ba'i dkyil 'khor lags te/ skye bo mang po las sman pa dang skye bo mang po la bde ba dang / 'jig rten la thug brtse ba dang
6a1(rgyud): skye bo'i tshogs chen po'i don du bdag lags na/ bshad du gsol dus gsum du gshegs shing bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// rang
6a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas dang 'phags pa nyan thos kyi dge 'dun 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang dang ltar byung ba thams cad la phyag 'tshalo// yang dag par song ba rnams dang yang dag par zhugs pa rnaMs la phyaga'o tshalo// sha ra dwa ti'i bu
6a3(rgyud): la phyag 'tshalo// byams pa la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'phags pa de bzhin gsheg pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
6a4(rgyud): 'od dpag med la phyag 'tshal lo// dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo// byang chub sems dpa' seMs dpa' chen po snying / rje chen po dang ldan pa 'phags pa spyan ras gzig kyi dbang phyug
6a5(rgyud): la phyag 'tsha lo// / tad+ya thA/ AM tsa ra tsa ra/ tsa ri tsi ri/ tsu ru tsu ru/ au ha hi ma hA ka ru na kA/ tsi ri tsa ri/ mi ri mi ri/ tsu ru tsu ru/ ma hA ka ru ni kA/ si ri si ri/ tsa ri tsa ri/ si ri pi ri/ bi ri bi ri/ ka le ma hA pad ma ha sta/ kA la kA la/ 
6a6(rgyud): kaM l-i ki laM/ ku lu ku lu/ mahA shud d+ha sadatwa/ b+hu d+ha b+hU d+h+ya/ d+hA prad+hA ga ka Na ka NA kri nu kai ShI kuNu ku tu/ pa ra ma shu d+ha/ pa ra ma shud+ha/ sad tra/ ka ra kA rA ki ri ki ri ku ru ku ru/ mat+ma s+thA ma snA ma/ tsa la tsa la/ sun tsu la/ bi tsi la e
6a7(rgyud): tram yonasu b+hai b+hapa/ b+hai d+hi/ b+hu d+harma / ke/ mArdzus shu ti she pa d+hi d+ha pa/ sa ras pa tsa/ 5 6/ m+bu \u0f7fg+h+ra ma k+Shar pram bi she d+ha d+ha ra/ d+hiri d+hi paM d+ha ru
6a8(rgyud): tang ga ter bags ras pa par nga la m-i sho tata pas drim na ti/ shin rjel dz+wal dzal/ ta bteb/ blag pam I ya byag+sas ku pir bra men gau/ de ba gni/ a pa bya skyed/ tsar nasanas tsun tsam su ru
6b1(rgyud): mu ru su ru su mu sod nang ku mu ru rung te/ b+ha sa b+hA b+hiSh+Tad+ha nAd pa ri shi nA ka ya/ bahU bi bi/ d+ha ba sha d+ha rad+ha d+ha ra/ d+hi rid+hi r-i d+hi ri d+hi raM/ d+hi ri d+hi raM d+hu ru d+hu ru/ tha ra tha ra g+ha g+ha re/ sa ra ya ra lA ra la ra/ ta ra ha ra/ ma ru mu ra/ sa ras
6b2(rgyud): ra pa ra ba ra/ ba ra d+ha ya ka/ sa man ta/ a ba lo ki ta/ lo ke shwa ra many+dza shwa ra/ mu hu mu h+ya/ mu ru mu ru/ ma ya ma ya/ mun tsa mun tsa// / bcom ldan 'das 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug bdag par sems can
6b3(rgyud): thams cad 'jigs pa thas cad dang gnod pa thams cad dang / 'tshe ba thams cad dang / gnod pa thas cad las bsrungs cig bsrungs cig/ gsad pa dang bcing ba dang / rgyal po dang chom rkun dang / me dang chu dang dug dang
6b4(rgyud): mtshan las yong su thaMs par mdzad pa/ ka rna ka NA kirni ki n+ya/ ku Nu ku N+ya/ tsa ra tsa ra/ i na tI ya pa ya/ b+ho d+ha kA tsa du ra/ ar+ya sad t+ye saM pa/ ka/ sha ta ka pa ta pa/ da ma da ma/ sa ma sa ma/ ma hA sa ta mon tA kra ra pi
6b5(rgyud): d+ha maM na 'dra pA dar mai ta pi ra ka/ mi li mi li/ ti ti Ta Ta/ dza dzaSh+pa tra/ Ta Ti Ti kr-i tsa tsan+da ma/ e ne ya tsa ra ma kri tra ri ka ra/ e h+ye he/ I shi ra ma he shra ma ra/ ma hA b+hu d+ha ga Na b+ha na tsa ka/ ku ru ku ru/ pa ra pa ru
6b6(rgyud): ka rA kA raM/ kaM Ta ka Ta/ ma Ta ma Ta/ bi shung+ga bi Sha/ sa ba si na ma hA ka ka ru ni kA/ shwo te ye de nyo pa bI ta/ rad na ma ku Ta/ mA lA d+ha ra/ sad rbad nya shi ra sa kI d+harma ku ta mA lA d+ha ra/ ma hI da bu ha ka mA lA la kri tai/ ka la ta la/ d+hA na sa
6b7(rgyud): ma d+hi bi mog sho a Ta ka ma bya/ sa hu sa ta ti pa ri pa ri tsa ka/ ma hA ka ru ni ka/ sarba karma a pa ra na b+hi shod+d+ha/ ka sarba bya d+hi bri mo tsa ka sarba a shwa pa ri su ra ka/ sarba sad tA sa ma shA sa ka na mo sU te swA hA/ 
6b8(rgyud): klags pas la su thams cad grub par 'gyuraro// dus gsum du bzlas brjod bgyid na/ 'tshams med pa lnga byang bar 'gyur zhing / las kyi sgrib pa thams cad kyang yongasu byang bar bgyid do// 'tshams med pa
7a1(rgyud): spyad pa la ni a ka ru 'dug pa'am/ thal ba'am chab pa'am/ yongs dkar dang / seng ldeng ge phur pA la sogs pas so// rims thams cad la ni bsrung paso// nad thams cad la ni ma ra ram 'bru mar
7a2(rgyud): che ba la bzlas brjod bgyis te gtor bar bgyi'o// byang bkrol ba la ni mtshon gyis so// lte ba la ni bsrungs pa'i skud pas samatsha chu so dug gsad pa la ni sa'am chab kyiso// mig nang la ni skud pa dkar pos rna ba la
7a3(rgyud): la btags par bgyi'o// son pa la ni shing kA ra ba ri'i so shing gris so// 'tshams bcad pa ni mtshon sna lnga'i skud pa la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas brjod bgyis te seng ldeng gyi phur pa bzhi lnga bcings na/ phyogs bzhir
7a4(rgyud): btsugs par bgyis na 'tshams chen po bcing bar bgyi'o// thams cad bsrung ba ni skud pa'am/ cheb pa'am thal bas so// gdon thas cang la ni mtshon sna lnga'i skud pa so// rims thams cad la ni srung
7a5(rgyud): bdakar po so// g.yan pa dang rdo dang / ldog pa dang mgrin pa 'ag/ ga pa thams cad la ni sbrang rtsi dang 'i pi ling sres so// mig nA pa la ni dri chu'am shing rta ra'i michus// rna ba'i nang la ni 'bru mar gyis so// 'ja
7a6(rgyud): dang gtsang ba dang 'gyed pa dang / skur pa 'debs pa thams cad la ni chab la bzlas brjod bgyis te la bshal par bar bgyi'o// dpung dang yul dang rgyal srid yul rnams bsrung ba la ni bum pa gang gzhag la
7a7(rgyud): la rtsang ma'am/ gos rtsang ma dgos pas mchod pa rgya chen por bgyis nas zhi ba chen por 'gyur ro// des yang chab kyis gter bar bgyi ste/ sems can thos cad bsrung ba bgyis par 'gyur ro// yam gyi
7a8(rgyud): nad dang gnod pa dang 'tshe ba thams cad zhi bar bgyi ba dang / blags blta ba rnams ni tsan don la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas/ brjod bgyi ste/ snying khar byug par bgyi'o// 'tshams ma mchis pa'i las thams
7b1(rgyud): cad pas bgyi ba la ni rtag tu bzlas brjod bgyi so// khyim bsrung ba la ni pad ma'i sbyin sreg bgyi so// sems can thams cad sbyang ba dang 'byung po'i 'jig pa dang / gdon thams cad las bsrung ba la ni tsan dan gyi sbyin
7b2(rgyud): sreg bgyi so// / dza ya dpa pi dza ya dang na ku li dang / g+han d+ha ku li dang / ba ru ni dang / tse 'dra 'du ni dang pa ri ni dang / a b+ha ya pe ni dang / i ni pra pa ni dang / g+han d+ha kri ya ku dang / rgya sres dang tsakra dang / ma hA tsa kra dang / bi stu tran
7b3(rgyud): ta dang / so ma ra dza dang / su nan da rnaM sa la lan brgya rtsa brgyad sbyin sreg bgyis te nor bur bgyis nas spyi bo 'am dpung pa la btags pa bsrel bar bgyi'o// khye'u rnams ni mgul par bgyi'o bu mo rnaMs la ni sta zur nA te/ dpal
7b4(rgyud): dang ldan par bgyid pa dang bkra mi shis pa rab tu/ zhi bar bgyid pa'i nor bu 'di bsrel na thams cad las bsrung ba bgyis par 'gyur ro// dug dang se mi tshig lags so// dug gi gnod pa bskyed par mi/ 
7b5(rgyud): 'gyu ro/ skye na yang gnod pa skyes par mi bgyid cis myur du zhi bar 'gyu ro// rlung dang ser ba gcod pa dang / char gyi rgyun dang ser ba zlog pa la naM shing ka ra ba ra'i lcug ma ste las thas cad bgyid pa/ 'phags pa
7b6(rgyud): spyan ras gzig kyi dbang phyug gi snying po grub pa dam pa ma bsgrubs pa ri las 'di rnams bgyid par 'gyur lag so// de nas bsgrubs par 'tshal na/ cho ga ni ras la lhag ma ma yin pa'i tshen rtsis sangs rgyas dang 'phags
7b7(rgyud): ba spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi gzugs brnyan ras pa'i thor tshug dang / e na ya'i lpags pa dang / phyugs bdag gi tshe lugs 'chang ba/ brgyan thas cad kyis brgyan pa bri bar bya ste/ ri mo mkhan gso sbyong can
7b8(rgyud): 'dri bar brtsal bar bgyi'o// de nas bsgrub po pos sku gzugs de'i spyan sngar zla khe do na de'i lce'i dkyil 'khor bgyis te/ me tog sil ma bkram la spos kyis bkang ba'i snod brgyad gzhag par bgyi'o// snod brgyad pa'o// 
8a1(rgyud): drug bcu rtsa bzhi'am/ gzhan yang lta bo shos sha dang khrag dang ma 'dres pa bshams shing 'dres la/ a ka ru'i gdug pas gdugs te/ lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjed 'gyi'o// nyin zhag gcig gam zhin
8a2(rgyud): zhag gsum du snang bar bgyis na/ zas dkar gsum du tshal te dus gsum du khras bgyis nas/ gos rtsang ma dgos nas/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug bdag nyid mchis nas/ bsam pa thas cad yongasu rdzogs
8a3(rgyud): par bgyidado// ldong ros sam/ mig sman la bzlas brjod bgyis te/ che mig la bskus na de mi snang bar 'gyuraro// na mkha' la 'chi bar 'gyur zhing don yod pa'i ya shes bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin thob par 'gyuraro// ci 'tshal
8a4(rgyud): bde bgyid par 'gyur ro// de ni bsgrub pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal na/ byang chub sems tha 'phags pa spyan ras gzig dbang phyag dang / gnas rtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag dang / mi 'byed kyi
8a5(rgyud): bdag po tshangs pa dang / dbang phyug dang dbang phyug chen po'i lha'i bu rnams yid rangs te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// / de bzhin gshegs pa rgya mtshor ba 'byam thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 
8a6(rgyud): de nas byang chub sems dpa' ses pa chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug stan las langs te/ bla gos 'phrag pa gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ nyi ma'i 'od ltar 'od zer stong 'pho zhing / 'od
8a7(rgyud): zer sna tshogs 'gyed pa'i lus bcom ldan 'das gang na de log su thal mo sbyar ba btud de zhal gyi dkyil 'khor rgyas shing rdzogs la zhing 'dzum pa'i gzhan gyis/ byams pa dang snying rje chen po'i mthu yid la byed pas rig bzhi'i 'jig rten
8a8(rgyud): la phan pa dang / snying rje bas don thos cad grub pa'i rigs sngags 'chang ba rnams kyis bla na med pa de kho na nyid grub pa mchog sbyin pa thob par bya ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag la
8b1(rgyud): don yod pa'i rgyal po'i cho ga zhib mo 'di mchis te/ 'di pad ma chen po'i rgyal po'i dkyil 'khor de kho na nyid chen pos 'phags pa'i snying por gyur pa de kha na nyid grub pa de dkyil 'khor 'di'i phyag rgya dang / gsang sngags dang snying
8b2(rgyud): po rim par phye ba gsang ba dam pa rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor dam tshig dam bsgrub pa gsang ba 'di bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar skrag par bgyi'o// lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / 
8b3(rgyud): mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i 'khor chen po'i 'dun du/ rig sngags bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'dun 'dir yang sbags par bgyi'o// gang yang dbang phyug dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / tshangs pa dang tshe lha dang gshin rje dang / chu lha dang
8b4(rgyud): lus ngan dang / drang srong gi tshogs dang / chu lha dang / zla ba dang / nyi ma dang / skar ma'i tshogs dang / rgyu skar dang rigs sngags 'chang grub pa'i lha mo rnams kyi mdun du de kho na nyid kyi snying po gsang ba dam pa skrag cing brjod par
8b5(rgyud): bgyi'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub ba bsod nams stong gi brgyan pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad rnams kyis rnam par spras pa/ phyag dpung pa'i mdog gser gyi kha dog lta bu'i 'od zer 'phro ba
8b6(rgyud): dra ma'i phreng ba dang / spos kyi glang po che'i sna lta bu'i phyag rgya ste/ byang chub sems thases dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi spyi bor gzhag nas klang ba la byugs te/ 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// sems
8b7(rgyud): can dag pa dam pa snying rje chen po dang ldan pa khyod smros shig/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis byin gyis rlabs pa gang gA'i klung byed ma 'bum phrag brgya stong gi bye ma'i rdul phra rab snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis kyang
8b8(rgyud): byin gyis rlabs shing / rjesu yid rang bar bgyi'o// de nas byang chub sems pa sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis phyogs bcur bltas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar rang gi de
9a1(rgyud): kho na nyid gsang ba'i sngags 'di dag gsol to// A~M pad ma a sta mahA a mo g+ha pa shA sa rta sa ma ya hra ta yan/ gis phyogs bcur bltas te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar rang gi tsa ra tsa ra
9a2(rgyud): hu'u ma don pa'i zhags pa'i rang bzhin gyis gzungs kyi snying po yin no// byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis gsang ba'i snying po 'di brjod ma thag tu/ ri'i rgyal po ta la
9a3(rgyud): 'di brag dang / nags tshul dang rtsi shing du bcas dang / ri rab khor yug dang khor yug chen po dang bcas pa rnams pa drug tu g.yos shing lha'i gnas rab tu ldeg par gyur to// thams cad 'dar 'drar por gyur to// 
9a4(rgyud): klu'i gnas dang gnod sbyin dang / srin po'i gnas rnams/ kyang 'khrugs par gyur te/ rtswamatsho chen po'i rlabs kyang 'khrug par gyuraro// rgyucher nas kyang 'khrug par gyur te// de ma thag tu
9a5(rgyud): bcu na sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan bzhugs pa rnams kyis leg so zhes bya ba byin te 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rgyal po'i bdag nyid du rnam skyes pa'i don yod pa'i gsang
9a6(rgyud): ba'i snying po klag pas grub pa bla na med pa smras pa legs so legs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas 'di skad ces bka' stsal pa/ sems dpa' dag pa khyod kyis gsang ba
9a7(rgyud): klags pa'i cho ga de nyid bsgrub pa rgyas pa dang bcas pa smros shig/ spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gsang ba'i snying po'i gzungs 'di lan cig brjod pa tsam gyis
9a8(rgyud): de'i mod la phyogs bcu tha dad nas/ gang gi klung sa ya brgya stong gi byed ma snyed kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag rkyang ste/ sbyin po la gzhag nas leg so zhes bya ba'i sgra gsungs te/ gsungs pa
9b1(rgyud): tsam gyi mod la/ sngon bskal pa brgya stong du bsags pa'i sgrib pa rnams nyams par gyur cig par bgyid do// sdug pa thams cad dang / nad thams cad dang / de bzhin du gnod pa zhi bar bgyid/ sems
9b2(rgyud): can gdug pa rnams dang / bas kyi rgol ba dang / mi 'jigs par bgyid de/ 'di la the tsom mi bgyi'o// rtag du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug mchod sbyin lta 'tshal bar bgyid lags so// 
9b3(rgyud): rigs 'di'i cho ga bsgrub pa ni 'di yin te/ rigs sngags 'chang rtsang bar gyur pas shin du khrus pa gyis te/ gos tsang mo bog par babya'o// byams pa dang snying rje yid la bgyis pas 'byung po zas
9b4(rgyud): cad la mchog tu snying bi rtse bar bgyi'o// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi ri mo'i sku gzugs la mchod par bgyi me tog dang btug pa dang / dri dang phreng ba dang / byug pa
9b5(rgyud): dang mar me 'bul bar bgyi'o// tshes brgya dam+ba bcoM lnga la/ bsgrub pa'i bzlas brjod kyi cho ga bgyi'o// ri mo'i gzugs kyi ma dun thog mar dkyil dkrung bcas la/ don yod pa'i
9b6(rgyud): zhag pa'i snying po lan brgya rtsa brgyad bgyi'o// tshag gzhan mi slu bar khro bo'i rgyal po brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis te/ chab dang yungs dkar gyi dbang bskur bar bgyi'o// phyag rgya bcing ba
9b7(rgyud): bya ste/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig tu bcing bar bgyi'o// bzlas brjod ston pa tsam gyis de'i mod la don pa'i zhag pa'i snying po khro bo'i rgyal po dang bcas pa'i bum 'gyur du bzlas brjod bgyis par 'gyur ro/ 
9b8(rgyud): bzlas brjod nas ri mo'i gzugs 'bar zhings yang g.yo bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi lus las 'od zer sna tshogs 'byung bar 'gyur ro// don yod pa'i
10a1(rgyud): nag pa'i snang po ri lag na thogs pa'i nag pa 'bar bar 'gyur ro// rigs sngags 'chang bar de srid dga' bar dang / spyi bo'i phyag 'bar bar 'gyur ro// 'di ni
10a2(rgyud): ni grub pa'i rtags yin no zhes bya ba'i rtags dang legs zhes byagyi ba'i byin te/ don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po'i cho ga zhi mo'i phyag rgya grub par 'gyur ro// de nas dgos pa thams cad
10a3(rgyud): dang las thams nAd dang / brjod pa tsam gyis de'i mod la grub par 'gyur lags so// de bzhin gshegs pa sa ya bye ba brgya stong gang ga'i klung gi bye ma dang mnyam pa'i gse
10a4(rgyud): gyi kha dog 'dra ba'i spyi bo'i rtag tu 'jogs/ pa rmi lam du mthong bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi rang bzhin gyi lus shin du dri ma dang
10a5(rgyud): bral yongs su dag pa dri ma med pa'i bdag nyid kyi lus kyi rang bzhin mdun du mchis par 'gyur ro// mchog thas cad brtsol bar 'gyur ro// don yod pa'i zhugs pa/ 
10a6(rgyud): snying po'i cho ga zhib mo'i phyag rgya grub pa brtsol bar 'gyur ro// ji ltar snying las skyes pa'i bu bzhin du sangs rgyas dang byang chub thob kyi bar du yongasu bskyong bar bgyid do// de bas
10a7(rgyud): na 'jig rten gyi khams bong ba can gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' dag yong su rdzogs pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing legs par brgyan pa byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba dang bca
10a8(rgyud): pa khang pa rtsegs ma legs par rgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri mchog la 'phags pa rgyal ba'i dpag med 'od zer brgya stong phrag 'bum 'phro ba'i sku bzhugs shing chos ston par 'tshal na/ 
10b1(rgyud): rigs sngags des legs par bkrus te/ rtsang mar gyur pas gos rtsang mar bgos te/ chos 'phrul gyi zla ba yar gyi ngol byams pa'i sems dang snying rje lhag pa'i bsam pas gus pa dang / 
10b2(rgyud): dang ba dang zhes dang bla mar bgyi'o// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi ri mo gzugs la ci 'byor pa'i me tog dang / gdugs pa dang / dri dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / 
10b3(rgyud): spos dang / lta ba lbu ba dang / ba dan gyis mchod par bgyi'o// tshes brgyad nas bcu gsum gyi bar du zas dkar gsum 'tshal bar bgyi'o// ri mo'i gzugs de nyid kyi mdun du nyin gtso/ 
10b4(rgyud): bzhin du yod pa'i snying zhag pa'i snying po lan nI shu rtsa gcig dang / tshig gzhan mi smra bar khro bo'i rgyal po lan nyi shu rtsagacig dang / snying po dang / nye ba'i snying po lan brgya
10b5(rgyud): brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis na/ ri mo'i gzugs de nyid kyi mdun du mchis nas nas nyal bar bgyi'o// mchod yin dang yon dang yon chab dus gsum dung bul bar bgyi'o// 
10b6(rgyud): a da kA ru dang / tsan dan dang / hu ru ka dang / gu gul dang / me tog gi khu ba dang / bcas pa bla rtsi dang / lhan cig bsregs nas spang bar bgyi'o// gdung ba'i sngag lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod
10b7(rgyud): bgyis te/ don yod khams gsum rnam par grags/ gdug pa'i rgyal po bla na med/ gang phyir gdug pa tsam gyis ni/ stong gsum gyis stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi phyog
10b8(rgyud): bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams su 'dug pa'i srin po 'khris pas rgyas par 'gyur ro// srin 'khrigs pa de dag gis sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems thams cad dang / lha dang klu dang
11a1(rgyud): gnod sbyin dang / dri zad pa lha ma yin dang / na mkha' ldeng dang / mi'am tsa dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa rnams la sri chen po'i mchod pa 'gyis par 'gyur zhing de dag
11a2(rgyud): thams cad dga' bar 'gyur ro// gang yang dud 'gro'i skye gnas su rtogs pa'i sems can gang dag gis gdug pa'i dri tshor ba dang / de dag thams cad ngan song du skye bar 'gyur ba'i las kyi sgrib pa
11a3(rgyud): rnams yongasu gdug par 'gyur ro// 'thab pa dang / 'thob mo dang / rtsod pa dang / 'gyed pa dang / 'tshang 'gru pa dang / 'khrug pa dang rmi lam ngan pa dang / yams nad dang / gnod pa dang / 'tshe ba dang / 
11a4(rgyud): gdung ba dang / me ge dang mi bde ba thams cad zhi bar 'gyur ro// rlung dang ser ba dang / grang ba dang tsha ba'i sprin thos cad zhi bar 'gyur ro// sdig pa thas cad 'jig par 'gyur ro// byad dang
11a5(rgyud): g.yengs byed dang / sngags kyi spyod pa thams cad dang / dug dang dbyig dang / dug sbyar ma thas cad zhi bar 'gyur ro// gdon thas cad dang rjed byed thas cad dang / rims dang bza' nye
11a6(rgyud): dang / 'og nyes dang gnod sgri pa dang / gnod ltas thas cad bdug pa'i dris 'dros par 'gyur ro// 'jig par 'gyur ro 'gyegs par 'gyur ro// byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du lan 'ga' yang
11a7(rgyud): tshugs par mi 'gyur ro// bdug pa'i rgyal po ni rtag tu sbyar bar bgyi'o// 'di ltar tshes bzhi'i nub mo mchis la don yod pa'i zhag pa'i snying po brgya rtsa brgyad dang / khro bo'i rgyal po'i rtswa rtsa brgyad zlas
11a8(rgyud): brjod bgyi'o// zas dkar gsum gyi rtor ma ci 'byor pa dbul bar bgyi'o// snying po dang nye ba'i snying po stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis la dri dang 'bru mar dbul bar bgyi'o// ri mo'i gzugs
11b1(rgyud): de nyid kyi 'dun tu nam langs kyi bar du mchis na nyal bar bgyi ste/ rmi lam dbyig gi mdzod mthong ngam/ bde ba can gyi 'jig rten gyi gzhal med khang dang bcas pa rin po che'i shing dang / rdzing dang gan
11b2(rgyud): dang khang pa brtseg ma dang bcas/ gzhal med khang la sogs pa rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul dang rnam pa dang bcas pa mthong ngam/ de bzhin gshegs pa la tshe dpag med byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyi
11b3(rgyud): bskor cing / khang pa rtseg pa na bzhugs pa lha dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri za dang lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang lto 'phye chen po 'khor dang / bcas pa mthong ngam/ bcom ldan
11b4(rgyud): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag/ par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag med de yang rig/ sngag 'chang de la dbugs byin par mdzad cing legs so/ 
11b5(rgyud): bgyi yang brtsol bar mdzad de/ kye skyes bu dam pa khyed kyis legs so rigs sngags 'tshang gyi skyes bu'i byed pa du ma byas pa dang / khyed kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mang du bskrun pa dang / khyod kyis lhag par
11b6(rgyud): mang du byas pa dang / khyod kyis bya ba gang yin pa byas pa dang / khyod don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor phyag rgya chen po dang / gsang sngags rnam par phye ba'i snying po bsgrub pa ni grub zan
11b7(rgyud): te/ legs so legs so// khyod rigs sngags 'chang gis sangs rgyas nyid du gyur cig/ khyod 'di nas ma 'ongs pa'i mngal gyi skye bu sbas te/ tshe rjes nas de'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skye bar 'gyur ro// byang chub kyi
11b8(rgyud): snying po la thug gi bar du sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro bar 'gyur ro// zhes phyag g.yas pa spyi bor 'jog par 'gyur/ 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub thams cad brtsol cing 'jig rten las 'das pa
12a1(rgyud): dngos grub grub ste/ 'di ni dam pa bsgrub pa yin no// zhes bdag nyid sad nas dga' ba mthong ste/ sgrub pa thams cad dang bral zhing yongs su dga' bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan
12a2(rgyud): ras gzigs dbang phyug bral ze'i gzugs kyis mdun na mchis pa 'gyur ro// zhing 'dod pa thams cad kyi mchog brtsol bar 'gyur ro// gzugs kyi ri ma de yang 'bar zhing 'od zera'abyung bar #
12a3(rgyud): ro/ yon tan rgya mtsho mang po gzhan yang thob par 'gyuraro// 'jig rten pa'i phun sum 'tshogs pa yang thob par 'gyur ro// skye bo dang brang ma ze dang / khyim bdag thas cad dbang du 'gyur zhing cher mchod
12a4(rgyud): par 'gyur ro// dge sbyong dang bram ze rnaMs las don yod pa'i bsgrub pa chen po thob par 'gyur// bsgrib pa chen po bla na med pa yang thob par 'gyur ro// nyin gcig bzhin du gsum du phyag rgya
12a5(rgyud): bcing bar bya'o// de nas tshes bcu bzhi la thob mar dag skyong dang bram ze rnaMs la ci 'byor pa'i yon dang bcas pa'i mchod ston bsngal ba bgyi'o// de nas bdag nyid longs spyad par bgyi'o// gang
12a6(rgyud): gi tshe yang sangs rgyas la lta ba dang / byang chub sems thal lta ba dang / lha rnams la lta bar 'tshal na de'i tshe badrug pa'i rgyal po la dgug pa'i gsang sngags lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas brjod bgyis te/ sangs
12a7(rgyud): rgyas bcom ldan 'das dgug par bgyi'o// dgug pa tsam gyi mdo la zhal ston par 'gyur zhing / dge ba'am mi dge ba thos cad dang nyams pa 'am 'bri ba de dag thams cad gsung bar 'gyur ro// ci tsam tshe'i ma
12a8(rgyud): cha thug gi bar du gsung ba'am/ 'gro ba'i 'ong ba gsung bar 'gyur ro// de nas gsang sngags kyi cho ga dang / bsgrub pa'i don dang las kyi cho ga yang ji lta ba bzhin bshang bar bgyi'o// oM ma d+ha rang
12b1(rgyud): a mo g+ha dzA ya de/ tsu ru tsu ru swA hA/ don yod pa'i rgyal po'i snying po'i gsang sngagaso// A~M pad ma pA sha d+hA ra a mo g+ha pa rang san tse da ya hUM/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang byang chub sems rba thams cad
12b2(rgyud): dang / lha dang klu dang gnod dang dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang mi dang mi ma yin pa la sogs pa bskal pa'i gsang sngags te/ bdug pa'i rgyal po btug nA/ 
12b3(rgyud): cha ba dang yungs kar bsres la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla brjod bgyes nas/ phyogs bcur rtor nas thas cad bskul ma bgyis par 'gyur ro// oM ma tra log kya a ba ha na/ a mo gA sha padam bi lo ka te/ a
12b4(rgyud): yA tu b+hu pa ni su ru su ru bi ma li hUM/ dgug pa'i gsang sngags te/ gu gul gyi dud pa lAn brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis na/ chu dang me tog sres pas phyogs bcur gtor bar bgyis
12b5(rgyud): te/ thas cad du bdugs pas dam pa grub pa legaso/ oM pad ma b+hu tsa mahA dza pa sha d+ha ri ni man tra ya mi/ A mo g+ha pa lA yan du b+hu ba sa ma ru mu ru hUM lAM/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang byang chub
12b6(rgyud): sems dpa' thams cad dang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang / dkyil 'khor thams cad na gnas pa'i lha tshogs la sogs pa spyan drang ba'i gsang sngags te rol pa spyi lugs dang / chab dang me
12b7(rgyud): tog dang tshems shing la bdug pa'i rgyal pos bdugs te/ thams cad la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis te/ thams cad spyan drang ba'i rig sngag so// oM pad ma a mo g+ha badz+ra a de ShA na ku ru kurtsa
12b8(rgyud): swAhA/ sa'i dkyil 'khor bcing ba ste/ chab dang yungs dkar la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis nas sa la rtor na dpag tshad sum rgyas kun nas 'khor ba'i sa 'i dkyil 'khor rdo rjer byin gyi rlabs
13a1(rgyud): par 'gyu ro// de thams cad bsrungs pas ni rdo rje sra ba'i semasu 'gyur ro// dgra rnams kyis mi mthong ba dang / bgegs dang log 'dren dang srin po dang / gnod sbyin dang sha za dang/ 'byung po dang / 
13a2(rgyud): rjed dang ro langs dang / 'dod dgur sbyar ba'i gzugs thams cad kyis mi mthong ste/ rnam pa thams cad du mi mthong bas rdo rje sra bar 'gyur ro// oM a mo g+ha sad sha mo du ra sau ha san du Ti/ saM ra~M sa~M ri d+hu ma
13a3(rgyud): gdan gyi gsang sngags sngags te/ yungs dkar la stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis te/ sal rtor na pad ma chen po'i gzhal med khang gi gdan du byin gyis rlabs nas legs par phul bar gyur ro// de bzhin
13a4(rgyud): gshegs pa thams cad la rin po che sna bdun las byas dpa'i seng ge'i bdan du byin gyis rlabs nas/ legs par phul bar bgyi'o// de rigs sngags 'chang gis stan la chab dang yongs dkar
13a5(rgyud): la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas brjod bgyis nas rtenate rigs sngags 'chang grub pa'i pad ma'i stan gsang ba'i gsang sngagaso// oM ma hA ka ru na/ pad ma a mo gA mo be sha dri badza at+ma
13a6(rgyud): Sh+ThA ta/ b+hu ru b+hu ru/ b+hu ru ban d+ha re swA hA/ dkyil 'khor mtha' dag na/ khyim dang nags tshal dang / kun dga' ra ba dang / rtsug lag khang dang sti gnas dang / 'chag sa dang / phug dang rgon pa'i gnas gsang ba'i phyir

18b1(rgyud): trai thilan/ nA rang ga bi b+ha ga ta yA/ sad sho d+had+ha trA swAr+tha/ mtshon ci'i gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas// oM bidir+ya a ba lo ga na~M/ ba~M b+ha dz+wa la du ba man nyen pa ma ra na swAhA/ lan nyi shu rtsi gcig bzlas
18b2(rgyud): brjod bgyis te/ so so rab kyi bar bgyi'o/ mA~M na ne pra hA ra na ma mo g+ha mAd tra/ dz+wa la dz+wa la sAhA/ phyag mtshan bri ba ste/ lan bdun bzlas/ oM ma a mo g+ha rang na sutra d+ha re kin ki ni sahA/ thig srung kyi gas
18b3(rgyud): sngags te/ lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod dkyil 'khor/ ri mo bri ba'i sngags sam/ gzhan ci yang rung ba la btab par bya'o/ A~M byai bu la dwe ri prA bai shA ya/ a mo g+ha pad me hUM/ sgra'i phyung bye ba ste/ 
18b4(rgyud): re rer yang lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// oM si b+hA ga/ te su ma ga la/ da ra b+ha ban ti/ AM dbyi b+hu dza na/ a mo g+ha ban shAn ban pa/ re gai raM gi r-i hU~M/ AM sa b+hUrnA ru bya dbyaM b+haM dzA nAM/ oM mo g+ha bad
18b5(rgyud): me sAhA/ lan bdun bzlas pa bgyi'o// AM pi bi d+ha ru ba ha ra pa ga ra na/ tsa la tsa la a mo gI taM swA hAM/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas sau/ AM daM pA bya ga na d+ha nu pa ri ni/ a mo g+ha b+ha le d+ha ra swA hA/ 
18b6(rgyud): mchod yon gyi gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlaso/ A~M g+ha na d+ha swar ni sa man d+ha/ oM mo g+ha pA s+phu ra hUM/ dri'i sngagasang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas/ AM ni ra ma la ka ya sho d+ha ni/ dib bA ga na d+ha pra pu ra
18b7(rgyud): ni pu ru ya hUM byug pa'i gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas so// A~M ding byA g+han d+ha pra pu ra naM sa ga ra dza la di ba bya/ a di Sha de ka la sho d+ha raM pur+Na pu ra yu dza sa d+hi swAhA/ bum pa'i dri chab kyi gsang sngags
18b8(rgyud): te/ lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlaso/ oM sa ra sa ra sa gra pa pa rbad ti bya d+ha/ de sa pu ra la hUM/ rtor ma ro sna tshogs can gyi gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas/ A di'i bya b+ho d+han saM bu ra ya/ 
19a1(rgyud): b+hi su la b+ha be swAm+ba/ kha zas kyi gsang sngags te/ lan ci shu rtsa gcig bzlas so// oM dr-i shAg kA b+ho rngan pa liM pa~M phul ra sa pra be se swa ra pra mur NAM/ zas dkar gsum gyi nor ma 'am/ gzhan la yang
19a2(rgyud): ldan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlaso// oM ba la ba tis rab ti ba bya ba swa taM/ tar da ma dus glu 'bras bu'i gsung sngags te/ lan bdun bzlaso/ mAM daMb byA ku su mo dpal nan pus/ ShApra pa re Sha ni b+hA ba swAhA/ me dog
19a3(rgyud): gi sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas/ oM b+hi ma lang+ga la ta pu Sh+pa kun hrid pa nas swa ti/ a ha ra saM pur+Na gr-i b+he swAhA/ me tog rto ba'i gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas// oM ma hA d+ha pa me g+ha pa
19a4(rgyud): la san tsA da ya sa man te hU~M swAhA/ dgug paraM/ gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlaso// oM a tha ra pa maM/ dz+wa la dz+wa la de mu khye swAhA/ me'i gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas so// 
19a5(rgyud): A ba khyau d+ha ma ni kan ka ra ni tha la b+hU dza ni/ ma da ma Ni a mo g+ha ma na~M sAp+na/ cha zhing brgyan pa'i sa gsang sngags te/ lan bdun pa zlas/ oM pad mo ka re bi ma la na kha a gu li sam sa ma/ sarba ta thA gaH
19a6(rgyud): a d+hI Sh+Ti tI sAhA/ thal mo sbyar ba'i rigs sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas so// oM sarba ku no than ta shi ro ba na yA na ma skA ro mi/ mi li mi li tsu ri ni sAhA/ phyag bgyi ba'i gsang sngags te/ lan bdun
19a7(rgyud): bzlas so/ oM sha rA daM shau a b+hi b+han d+ha na pa rA dud+h+we/ skor ba'i gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// oM b+haM b+haM d+ha yud d+ha dza lI ta pa ni pA s+yA ra h+ne/ thal mo'i sngags te/ AM di ba bya ma mo gA pa pU
19a8(rgyud): la sre re d+ha ra ni ri g+ha sha~M ru te// ra na ra Na~MhUM/ dril bu'i gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas so// yang na brgya rtsa brgyad do// oM ra sh+ma dz+wa la saM mni tan a ba b+has ma yi mnyam ni d+ha na ni khyi swAhA/ 
19b1(rgyud): mar me rigasang sngags te/ lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlaso/ oM d+hu ru d+hu ru a ba ha ya shig+hA dz+wa bed+d+he/ dgug pa ri gsang sngags te/ gu gul gyi bdug pa la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas// oM tuSh+Ta sad d+hA ba~M bo d+ha Ni sa ma
19b2(rgyud): sa mA ya bi ri swA hA/ dam tshig gi gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas so// oM bi tsa tri pa bu la pra pa ra d+ha ni hUM/ bgrang phreng gi gsang sngags te/ lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlaso/ oM bi tsi tra ra/ rad na dza
19b3(rgyud): la di ba bya ku su me ma ba re ShA ra ti swA hA/ me tog phreng da ba'i gsang sngags te/ lan btun bzla so/ oM dibi bya la tsa ni a g+ha pra ra ri sarba byaMd r+ya a d+haMSh+ThA na si de shu d+hi pa baM lo ki ti sAng+ga/ dgug
19b4(rgyud): pa'i gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gsum bzla so// AM a mo g+ha pa ra me sa man ta shu b+hA naM/ ta ra da ra gang dza saM b+ha naM swA hA/ slar gshegs gsol pa'i gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa
19b5(rgyud): gcig bzla so// oM da bi bya sa ma pu ra Ni N+ya ga bi lo ka ni hU~M/ khA ra sil gyi gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// AM pa de mo pra pu ra yang a mo g+ha ba ti pa man ta pra b+he swA hA/ lhung gzed kyi gsang
19b6(rgyud): sngags twe/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// au tu ra b+ha s+tha ra b+hi d+ha a d+hi ShA ta pra ba raHsu ru su ru ri shi su dza ti sA hA/ rtsa ding ba'i gsang sngags te/ la naM nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// AM dza la tu ma dza la du ma
19b7(rgyud): dz+wA la shaM khyer shr-I gar b+he swAhA/ sbyin sreg gsang sngags to/ lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlaso// oM pad mo ni pad ma sa ni ba rang pra ba re ni swA hA/ 'bab chu dang mtsho ri gsang sngags te/ lan bdun bzlas/ 
19b8(rgyud): oM khadag tsAr ni ga ma ga ma ya pra da pra tsa rin n+d+ra/ len pa'i gsang sngags te lan brgyartsa brgyad bzlas/ A~M sarba tram mo b+ha d+haM shi ka chung nga ba'i ma le a b+hi shin tsa tu man pra ba ni b+hu dza bad ma tA dza sar+b+ba/ 
20a1(rgyud): dbang skur pa'i gsang sngags te/ lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzla so// rig sngags 'chang gis gsang gas 'di dag thams cad so sor cho ga zhib mo'i cho ga bsgrub pa ji lta ba bzhin du thams cad so sor
20a2(rgyud): sbyar nas cho bsgrubs na/ dgos pa rgya chen po 'byor pa'i mthu chen po 'di dag dang / me tog dang 'dug pa dang / dri dang phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / rin po che'i snod sna tshogs dang / nor bu sna tshogs kyi gzhal
20a3(rgyud): maud khang chen blo 'byung bar 'gyur ro// lha'i me/ tog dang bdug pa dang / ba dan sna tshogs pa 'byung bar 'gyu ro/ ro brgya dang / ldan pa'i kha zas kyi mchog dang / ro tshogs kyi rnam par 'byung
20a4(rgyud): bar 'gyu ro// tsa tsam de bzhin gshegs pa la 'os pa'i gzhal med khang rnams 'byung bar 'gyu ro// byang chub sems dpe'i gzhal med khang rnams ji lta ba'i de lta bu dag 'byung bar
20a5(rgyud): 'gyu ro// klu rnams dang gnod sbyin rnams dang / lha ma yin rnams dang / nam mkha' lding rnams dang / mi 'am ci rnams dang / lto 'phye chen po rnas kyi so so gzhal med khang ji lta bu de dag 'byung bar 'gyur
20a6(rgyud): mi rnams kyi khang pa ji lta ba dang / kha zas kyi mchog de lta bu dag 'byung bar 'gyuraro// de lta bas na dgos pa rnam pa thams cad dong de kho na nyid bsgrub pa ji skad gsungs pa'i cho ga zhi ba mo dang
20a7(rgyud): ga dang gsang sngags bsgrub pa rnams 'gyu'o// de nas rigs sngags 'tshang gi bsgrub pa bla na med pa thams cad thob par 'gyuraro// gal te rig sngags 'chang gi las thas cad yongasu rdzogs par
20a8(rgyud): 'gyim te/ don yod pa'i zhig pa'i snying po 'di brjod pa tsam gyis rig sngags 'chang gi'i dun tu bdag rang gi gzugs nye bar mchis nas/ bsam pa dang ra ba thams cad yongs rdzogs par bgyi'o// sdig
20b1(rgyud): ba dang gnod pa thams cad 'jig par 'gyi'o/ yongasu dag pa'i rgya chen po ltar lus dag par bgyi'o// cho ga zhi mo dang phyag rgya dang gsang sngags dang snying po dang dkyil 'khor dang don yod pa'i rgyal po
20b2(rgyud): rnam par dkyil 'khor grub pa'i mchog thas cad brtsal bar bgyi'o// rig sngags 'chang 'khor lo bsgyur ba chen po'i dbang skur bar bgyi'o// de kho na nyid yang dag par bsgrub pa 'grub par brtsal bar
20b3(rgyud): bgyi'o// don yod pa'i zhag pa 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa bsgrub pa'i grub po rtsal bar bgyi'o// shin du rgya che zhing bag tshal ba ma mchis pa dang / mchod pa dang bkur bsti chen po 'dza/ 
20b4(rgyud): rten zas cad kyi mchog khyad par 'phag shing nor 'du ngon/ dkra shis dang dpal brtsal bar bgyi'o// 'di la yid gnyis dang so nye skyed par mi bgyi zhing / dngos po gzhan du yid la mi bgyi zhing / 
20b5(rgyud): sems can thas cad la byis pa dang / snying rje dang dga' ba dang / btang snyoms kyis brtse ba la mchog tu brtson par bgyi'o// bu cig pa bzhin du sems can du gyur pa thas cad la mchog tu brtse bar bgyi'o// bden
20b6(rgyud): bar smra ba dang bden pa la dga' ba dang / snyan par smra ba dang skang rjes lhag pa'i bsam pas dmigs na/ don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po bzlas par bgyi'o// bzlas brjod kyi cho ga bgyi zhing phyag rgya dang gas
20b7(rgyud): sngags kyang bzlas par bgyi'o// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du rtog pa ring bzhin gsheg pa rnaMs yid la bgyis na/ sangs rgyas rjesu dran pa sgom par bgyi'o// sangs rgyas dang byang chub seMs mthas
20b8(rgyud): la phyag 'tshalo// 'phag pa mogan po spyan ras gzig dbang phyug la phyag 'gyis na mngon sum du bcas par bgyi'o// bco ldang 'phag pa spyan ras gzig dbang phyug gi ri mo'i gzug la phyag 'gyi'og/ mdun na rtsa'i
21a1(rgyud): gding ba btang nas/ dkyil mo dkrung bcas te mchis nas/ gzhan mi smra bar bzlas pa bgyis te/ 'di ni gsang ba'i de kho na nyid bsgrub pa'o// de nas phyag rgya dang gsang sngags brjod par bgyi'o// 
21a2(rgyud): bdag la don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po'i de kho na nyid grub par gyur cig/ 'jig rten dbang phyug mgon po thug rje can/ sems can la byas pa sems dpa' dag/ lag na pad ma sos can thas cad la byis pa'i
21a3(rgyud): bdag nyid can gyis byin gyis brlos kyis/ phyog bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa kun dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / srid po lha min gsang ba pa/ 'jig rten skyong ba tshangs pa dang / drag pa khyab
21a4(rgyud): 'jug gzhon nu sogs/ gshin rje chu lha lus ngan dang / drang srong tshogs dang de bzhin du/ zla nyid kun bgyid gzhon nu dang / de bzhin dbang phyug tshe dbang bdag phyag rgya bcings pa tsam gyis ni/ 
21a5(rgyud): de dag myur tu grub par 'gyur// sgrol ma mdun ni 'du bar 'gyur/ de bzhin pha rol phyin bcu dang / mgrin sngon de bzhin gos dkar can/ de bzhin pad ma gar gyi dbang / rgyal dang rnam rgyal nyid
21a6(rgyud): dang mi lcog sgeg rdo rje lcag dang / lha mo 'khro gnyer ma ma kyi/ dpal mo pho nyi mo dang ni/ 'jig med dpal dang byangs can dang / pad ma kun 'di ud pa la/ pad ma'i so can de bzhin du/ ti se'i ni rtse me na/ 
21a7(rgyud): 'phrog ma'ibyung po'i ma dge dang / de bzhin lag na rdo rje bcu/ mthu chen ci bzhin rigs 'dzin dbang / rdo rje 'chang chen de bzhin du/ bcu gsum lha dbang lhan cig dang / sum bcu gnyis gnas lha dag na/ gas
21a8(rgyud): sngags phyag rgyas bcings tsam gyis// de dag zas cad 'du bar 'gyur/ phyogs bcu'i di bzhin gsheg pa thas cad kyis rnam par gzigs shing ston par mdzad do// de'i mad la byang chub seMs za rnas kyi/ 
21b1(rgyud): rna bar gzigs shing rtag tu mchog brtsol bar 'gyuraro// rtag tu mgon po spyan ras gzig dbang phyug phyag stong spyan stong pa/ phyag sna tshogs pa 'dzin pa lta 'tshal bar 'gyi'o// phyag rgya bcings pa tsam
21b2(rgyud): gyis ni/ bram ze'i cha lug don yod zhag/ mthong bar 'gyur te the tsom med/ mgrin ston dang ni rta mgrin dang / de bzhin rgya mtsho'i gling dang ni/ mgon po zhal ni bcu gcig dang / de bzhin zhal ni bzhi dag dang / 
21b3(rgyud): mogon po 'jig pa brgyad 'phrog dang / de bzhin 'jig pa bsam mi khyab/ snang ba sna tshogs gzug dang ni/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ding 'dzin dang / phyag rgya bcings pa tsam gyis ni/ mogan po thos cad ston par mdzad
21b4(rgyud): bde ba can gyi 'jig rten khams/ rgyal ba 'dren pa 'od/ dpag med// byang chub ses pa'i tshogs bskor ba/ mgon po mod la mod la mthong bar 'gyur gzhan yang sangs rgyas zhing ni stong
21b5(rgyud): dag dang / bya chu bo ga dga'i bye ma dang / mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa 'bum// bye ba brgya phrag spong rnaMs la/ byang chub seMs dpa'i tshegs bcas yongasu skor mgon phyag rgya bcings
21b6(rgyud): pa tsam gyis mthong bar 'gyur/ mthong ba chen po rna pa gzhan mthong ste/ nyin gcig bzhin du byang chub snying po dang / chos kyi 'khor lo rdo rje gdan/ de dag rmi lam snang bar mthong bar 'gyur/ de la yid
21b7(rgyud): gnyis so nyi the tsam med/ sangs rgyas rnaMs kyis gshung ba'am mtshams med lnga/ mgon po de la gdug sems nyid dang ni/ byang chub seMs dpa'i bar chad 'phags pa la/ kha zor nyid dang dam chos
21b8(rgyud): smra ba dang / rgyal ba'i mnar med gzhol ba dang / mi bzad dmyal ba bcu drug gnas pa dang / bskal pa 'bum tshe thas cad skad cig grol/ phyag rgya gsang sngags bzlas pa tsam gyis 'am/ thos sam mtho
22a1(rgyud): ngam ming ni bzung bas kyang / sdig pa de kun 'jig 'gyur the tshom med/ don yod nags snying phyag rgya mthong ba yang / 'jig rten mgon dang mtshungs te khyab par 'a'ag/ sangs rgyas 'dum
22a2(rgyud): phrag stong dang gang ga'i/ bye ba brgya steng dag ni mthong bar 'gyur/ byang chub snying por dgos pa thams cad dang / chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar 'gyur/ don yod zhags pa'i snying po phyag rgya dang
22a3(rgyud): gsang sngags mthong na bsod nas phung chen gyi/ bsod nams phung po 'di dag 'jal bar 'gyur/ de'i tshe yang rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur/ de ni dpag tu med par sem nyi med/ de nas rigs
22a4(rgyud): gsang 'chang brtsang gyur nas/ rtsang ma'i gos bgro nas ni thog mar yang / yo byad bsgrub pa rtsang spyod pa rtsang / rtag tu yan lag spos ni sna tshogs dang / sna tshogs gdugs pas
22a5(rgyud): rab tu bdug bgyis shing / dpung pa lag pa lha'i spos kyi se byugs/ rtsang ma'i sa phyogs rtsang ma'i gdan bshams par/ dkyil mo dkrung bcas nas ni byis pa sems dang / snying rje'i lhag pa
22a6(rgyud): bsam pa bsam pa de nyid mnyam gzhag nas/ phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas dang / rtag tu 'jig rten dbang la phyag rgya zhing / rtag tu bla ma mchod nas chos la brtson shin tu rig pas
22a7(rgyud): tshatshig gzhan mi smra bar/ shin tu rig pas bsrung ba'i cho ga bgyi/ shin du bkra shing bla ma de nyid gus/ bden par smra zhing snyam par smra ba dang / sems can kun la snying rje'i bdag nyid can/ lhan cig rjes mthun
22a8(rgyud): gyur nas de dag ni/ phyag rgya 'di bcings par gyur te/ lag pa nyi ma'i tshul du gzhag la sor mor nas/ mnyam par bcings te mthe chung zla ba'i tshul du snying khar gzhag go/ phyag rgya 'di ni don yod pa
22b1(rgyud): rgyal ba'i snying po'i rtsa ba'i phyag rgya ste/ byang chub kyi snying po'i bar du rtsol bar bgyid do// mgon po 'jig rten dbang phyug dgug pa'i gsang sngags 'di brjod do// oM a mo g+ha pa ku ra di pi ta sa man ta a
22b2(rgyud): pa lo ka ya man te'i ya tA/ a d+hiSh+ThA ta a mo g+ha pad me tsa ra sa na tsa raM hUM huM/ de ma thag tu dus gsum du rnam par lba po don yod pad dma' bar/ gsal ba'i cha 'phrul dang bcas pa'i phyag rgya'i rgyal pos
22b3(rgyud): shin du phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i dus gsu hu ga sheg pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing mang po mtha' dag cher g.yo bar 'gyur ro// dus gsurutu gshegs shing bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
22b4(rgyud): de dag gi sku las 'od zer sna tshogs 'bum phrag/ brgya stong du ma byung nas/ de bzhin gsheg pa de dag thas cad rab tu dges shing / sangs rgyas kyi yid la mdzad pa'i thugs rje chen pos
22b5(rgyud): phyag gser gyi mdog lta bu rkyang nas/ rigs sngaga'achang gi spyi bor 'jog par mdzad do// grub pa dam pa don yod pa rnam par sprul pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa brtsol par 'gyur ro// dbang phyug
22b6(rgyud): de dbang phyug chen po dang / tshangs pa dang lha'i bu dang / gshin rje dang chu lha dang / lus ngan dang khyab bdag dang kun 'byed dang / gzhon nu la sogs pa lha rnams bsrung ba dang / skyob pa dang sbed par 'gyed par

22b8(rgyud): thas cad bgyod pa'i phyag rgya thas cad du mchog las par gragos pa lag so// don yod dam tshig mchog grags pa/ pad ma rgyas pa'i phyag rgya ba cing / 'dzub mo gong mo rnaMs pad ma lcags kyu'i tshul du bgyi// 
23a1(rgyud): sor mo mnyam par gzhag pa'i phyag rgya 'di stan te/ rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor rtse ba'i phyag rgya 'dzin pa'i gsang sngags 'di brjod do// oM a mo g+ha pad ma gug sha sa ma ya naM/ gr-i b+ha gr-i b+ha/ 
23a2(rgyud): d+ha ra d+ha ra ma hA sa tA hUM/ phyag rgya bcings te bcings ma thag tu'am/ bzung ba tsam gyis dus gsum du gsheg pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnaMs kyis leg so zhes bgyi ba la sogs par 'gyur ro// 
23a3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thas cad dge pa dang / mnyes pa dang rab tu dges pa dang / tsham pa dang thugs dges pa skye bar 'gyur zhing ri gus sngags 'tshang la thugs rje chen po rgyas pa'i snying po grub pa dam/ 
23a4(rgyud): pa rtsol bar 'gyur zhing / yang nas yang du mthong bar brtsol bar 'gyur ro// mchod pa thas cad brtsol bar 'gyuraro// don yod/ pa'i zhags pa'i dam tshig grub pa brtsol bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin
23a5(rgyud): gshegs pa gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga zhig mo'i phyag rgyad dang / gsang sngags sngags 'dzin pa rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor bzung ba tsam gyis dam tshig rjesu 'jug par 'gyur ro// thas
23a6(rgyud): cad du 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor phyag rgya dang dam tshig 'tshal par 'gyu ro/ thams cad du dgongs pa'i gsang sngags grub par 'gyu ro// 'phags
23a7(rgyud): pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug mchog sbyin po rtag tu lta bar 'tshal bar 'gyu ro// lag 'thil pad ma ltar bgyis la 'dzub mai rje ltar bgyis zhing / mthe'u rlung rkyang phyag ni/ bang ma 'tshang la 'dug/ 
23a8(rgyud): pa dang me tog la sogs dri rnaMs dang / phreng ba byug pa phye ma dang / bdan gos dang rgyan dang ni/ ma mchod yon rab tu dbul/ buM pa gang ba dri sogs dang / mtshon yang zas ni sna tshogs la/ phyag rgya
23b1(rgyud): 'di ni dbul ba'i phyag rgyar gsungs/ zas cad du ni don yod mchog cho gar brgyad pa'i phyag rgya 'di/ pad ma'i phyag gis byin gyis brlabs// gong mo nor bu lta bu bsris pa'i phyag rgya 'di// 
23b2(rgyud): bag tsha med pa'i pad ma rin po che'i phyag rgya lags te/ 'di ni grub pa dam pa lag so// spyan bgrad pa'i gsang sngags ni/ A~M oM mo g+ha pad ma/ ma hA sad tra yan du ma hA ma Na ta le/ pi ri pi ri pad ma
23b3(rgyud): b+hu dza swA hA/ du sa gsum gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas rnaMs gsol ba btab po gsang spogs te/ byang chub sems rba thams cad dang / phyag na pad ma gsol btab dgug/ lha rnams kun dang de
23b4(rgyud): bzhin du/ dkyil 'khor gyi ni lha rnams dgug phyagargya 'di ni bcings pa yis/ phyog bcu kun gyi sangs rgyas dang / de/ bzhin byang chub sems rba 'dra/ lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang
23b5(rgyud): dri za lha min de bzhin du/ na mkha' lding dang mi 'am ci/ 'phye chen po nyid dag ste/ de kun skad cig 'du'agyur zhing / bsrung ba'i phyir na som nyi med/ lag na rdo rje'i tshul tu gzhag/ lhag pa'i mthon
23b6(rgyud): chung rnas pad ma'i tshul tu byas te/ gong mo rnas yud tsam bkug pa'i phyag rgya bcings pa ni grub ldan 'di ni bcings dbang gis/ 'khor bcing bar bgyi'o// bsrung ba'i las la bag cha med/ phyag rgya
23b7(rgyud): med ni bcings tsam dang / gosang sngags stong ni bzlas tsam gyis/ dpag tshad bdun me 'kho yug rje 'tshams bcings dkyil 'khor ba dang / bsrung ba'i las ni bgyes par 'gyur/ A~M oM mo g+ha
23b8(rgyud): badz+ra da d+ha pad ma b+han d+ha sa man te na/ ma hAs man bge shin tu man/ tsu ru tsu ru swAhA/ de nas snod phyag rgya ste grub ldan seMs deng 'acan kun sman pa/ don yod pa'i phyag rgya ni/ khyad par 'phags pa gnan yang
24a1(rgyud): yang stan/ rdo rje thal mo sbyar nas sor mo rnams mnyam par gnags ste/ srin lag kha gdengs la sor mo rnams yid tsam smras pa ni/ don yod sna tshogs rgyal po yi// pad ma'i phyag rgya chen
24a2(rgyud): bor grags/ phyag rgya 'di ni las kun dang / 'jug pa'i las kun sbyar ba rang dkyil 'khor phyag rgya mchog kun gsums// phyag rgya 'di ni bzung tsam na/ gsang sngags dam pas bsrung bgyis nas rigs
24a3(rgyud): sngags 'chang bar 'jug par 'gyur// dus gsum gsheg pa rnam thar pa'i/ dkyil 'khor ngam pa grub par 'gyur/ A~M badz+ra badz+ra A d+hiSh+Tha na pad me b+h+ye sha ru ba d+ha re/ d+ha ra d+ha ra hUM/ pra be sha du sta'u yang/ 
24a4(rgyud): d+ha g+ha d+ha g+ha d+ha d+han d+hi ri ru de swAhA/ phyag rgya 'di ni bcings de tsam gyis/ de nyid grub pa'i phyogs bcu la/ sangs rgyas zhing ni drug tu/ g.yo bar 'gyur bar som nyi med/ phyag na pad mo lus
24a5(rgyud): 'bar nas/ mgu ba chen po 'byung bar 'gyur/ rig/ sngogs 'chang ba 'dzub bzhin gyis/ rten tu lta zhing mdun na mtshas sangs rgyas kyi ni zhing kun dang / mtho ris sgo nas 'byed par 'gyur/ 
24a6(rgyud): sum bcu rtsa gnyis gnas rnas na/ gnas pa'i lha rnaMs sgo 'byed cing / sum bcu rtsa gsum gnas sgon/ gan pa thas cad sgo byed do// bde chen 'jig rten mkhas dag gi/ smon gan pa ste 'byed do// phyag rgya'
24a7(rgyud): ni bcings tsam gyis/ gnas kun du ni 'jug par 'gyur/ phyag rgya sdig pa thas cad 'phrog/ nye ba'i nyon mongs thas cad 'joms/ sdug bsngal kun las rnam par grol/ gnod pa thas cad 'jog par bgyid/ dmya
24a8(rgyud): ba bcu drug gnas las thar/ phyag rgyas bcings pa tsam gyis na/ mi bzang 'jig pa brgyad rnaMs dang / nye byas thas cad 'jig par bgyid/ dmyal ba'i sgo rnas bcad par 'gyur/ mi bzad 'jig pas sprul bar 'gyur/ 
24b1(rgyud): phyag rgyas bcings pa tsam gyis ni/ mi bzad brgyad rnaMs dang / nyes byas thas cad 'jig par bgyid/ dmyal ba'i sgo ni bcad par 'gyur/ mi bzang 'jig bsgral bar 'gyur/ phyag rgya 'di ni mthong tsam gyis
24b2(rgyud): 'tshams med lnga ni bgyis pa ni/ sdigs pa kun las rnam par tha ra/ sems can kun la rtag tu sdug/ de bzhin gsheg kun byin gyis rlob/ phyag rgya 'di nyid ni mtho bong gi/ rtse mo cung zad bkug la bzung ste/ 
24b3(rgyud): gong mo ril ba'i tshul du bgyis te/ spyi bo'i ral pa gzhag pa ni/ padad+ma pa ral pa'i phyag rgya lags te/ 'di ni don yod pa'i lag pa zhes sbags te/ sems can zas cad la phan pa'i slad du gsang sngags 'di
24b4(rgyud): brjod par bgyi'o// A a mo g+ha pad mdza le bi shad ya hUM/ bi ri bi ri ma le swA hA/ phyag rgya spyi bor gzhag nas chab gyis bsrungs nas gsang sngags ni/ brgya rtsa brgyad du zlas na su/ phyag rgya gas
24b5(rgyud): sngags dogs med pas/ rtag tu rkus pa'i mod tsam gyis/ mi rtsang ba ni rtsang bar 'gyur/ mi rtsang spyod pa rtsang ba dang / tshangs spyod ma yin tshangs spyod 'gyur/ mi thug pa ni thub par 'gyur/ lha
24b6(rgyud): rnaMs kun ni 'du 'gyur te/ bsrung ba'i phyir ni som nyi med/ mgon po 'a 'ag pa spyan ras gzigs/ seMs dpa' mchog sbyin dag pa'i/ mchog sbyin rgyun du thas cad rtsa/ nyi ma rer mthong 'gyur zhing / tshe 'phel rtag tu na
24b7(rgyud): 'gyur/ de bzhin dgu dang rgyas par 'gyur/ thas cad du ni las 'grub ste/ gnod pa kun las rnam par gro gra// sgrub pa rnaMs las rnam par thas cad du ni bkra shis mchog/ khrus kyi dam pa 'di dag ni/ don
24b8(rgyud): yod khrus kyi mchog yin no// lag gnyis sngams la 'og tu bstan/ srin lag gnyis yid tsam skums pa ni/ pad ma'i nor bu lags te/ kun kyang de ni mnyam par gzhag/ phyag rgya ting 'dzin lta bu 'di/ 
25a1(rgyud): dkyil mo daglang bcas mchis na su// phyag rgya 'di dag ba cing bgyis zhing / mnyam par gzhag nas gsang sngags bzlas/ bcings pa tsam gyi mod nas ni/ dkyil krung rdo rje lhun mnyam 'gyur/ kun nA
25a2(rgyud): go char gyur nas ni/ bgegs dang log 'dren thas cad dang / gnod sbyin srin po 'byung por bcas/ lha min na mkha' lding mi mthong // phyogs dang phyogs 'tshems rnam dag tu/ de dag thas cad rgyang ring bros/ bgag
25a3(rgyud): med par ni las 'grub pas/ bzlas pa'i las la som nyi med/ oM a mo g+ha dza dz+nyA d+ho bid ma shwa ra hUM/ thal mo mnyam par sbyar la/ 'dzub mo dang gung mo bkug nas/ mthe bo pad ma kha phye ltar bgyis te/ don yod dbang
25a4(rgyud): phyag rgyal po'i phyag rgya'o// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ dbang phyug gi mdun tu gsang sngags dang / phyag rgya bar cing bar bya'o// oM pad me shwa ra/ a mo g+ha ba ra d+ha/ b+ha ri b+ha ra swA hA/ 'di thog mar
25a5(rgyud): bzlas brjod nyi shu rtsa gcig bgyi'o// de'i 'og tu phyag rgya bcings nas/ don yod pa'i zhag pa'i de kho na nyid sems pa yi/ bas pa rtseg cig pas bzlas brjod bgyi'o// lan cig bzlas pa
25a6(rgyud): tsami gyis mo la dus gsum du rgyun du gshegs pa'i sangs rgyas 'bum phrag brgya stong gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed dang mnyam par g.yo bar 'gyur zhing / de bzhin gsheg pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzog
25a7(rgyud): pa'i sangs rgyas rnas kyis rig sngags 'chang de la leg so zhes bgyis pa brtsol bar 'gyuraro// dbugs 'byin par mdzad do// rig sngags 'chang la 'od zer sna tshogs rtog par mdzad do// mgon po spyan ras
25a8(rgyud): gzig dbang phyug dran par babyis pa tsam gyis mod la mdun du mchis par 'gyur ro// 'di ltar bcings pa tsam gyis pha rol du phyin pa drug yongasu rdzogs par 'gyu ro// pha rol tu phyin pa bcu dang ldan par 'gyur
25b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bcwo brgyad dang ldan par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gsheg pa'i stobs dang ldan par 'gyur ro// mi 'jigs pa bzhi thob par 'gyu ro// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad
25b2(rgyud): pa yong su dag pa thob para' gyuraro// phyag rgya bcings la don yon pa'i rgyal po'i snying po dran pa tsam gyis mod la yon tan dang phan yon rnaMs thob par 'gyur ro// bzlas brjod brgya rtsa brgyad bgyis la
25b3(rgyud): phyag rgya lan brgya brgyad bcings nas zhag cig sbyang bar bgyis ste/ bzlos brjod pagyis na/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang bdag nyid rang bzhin du mdun du mchis nas/ rig sags 'chang la
25b4(rgyud): leg so leg so// 'di ni bzlas brjod 'gyid pa yin no// da zhes dpung pa g.yas pa rkyang ba'i lag pas rig sngags 'chang gi spyi/ bor gzhag nas dbug 'byin par 'gyur te/ tshur shog bu gang
25b5(rgyud): 'dod pa'i mchog slongs shing dang sbyin no// khyod rjesu bzung zhing byin gyis rlabs pas/ nga'i bu rig sngags 'chang gi mthu bor gyur cig/ rig sngags 'chang khyod kyis don yod pa'i zhag pa sgrubs
25b6(rgyud): pas na rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgya rim par byed pa dang / cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal rten par bgyis shig/ snying rje chen po'i sas can thos cad la goms par gyis shig/ khyod 'di nas ma 'ongs pa'i
25b7(rgyud): mngal tu gnas shing 'phos ste/ 'jig rten gyi khas bde ba can du 'gro bar 'gyur zhing / khyod pad ma'i nang tu rdzus de skyes nas/ rgyan thas cad kyis rgyan cing mtshan dang dpe byad rab tu rgyan pa/ byang chub kyi ska
25b8(rgyud): po'i mthar thug gi bar du tshe dpag tu med par 'gyu ro// 'di ltar tshig gzhan mi smra bar lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod bgyis te/ lan stong rtsa brgyad tshang na/ na mkha' la mchi bar 'gyur ro// don yon pa
26a1(rgyud): nga d+hA sprul pa / rje zla gang 'i min nga rten pa'i 'dzig rten gyi ma dang bskams pa las rgyang du tsam gyim mchin sa bldon pa // 
26a2(rgyud): dbus brjod pa rgya stong dbyis pa/ thig tu slong bcings na tshe 'ad pa la 'phags paspyan ras gzigs dbang phyug 'dra bar 'gyus/ sgyum la bu'i dang 'dzin gyis rnam par rol padzi ngan yod pa
26a3(rgyud): mig yongasu dag par thob par 'gyuraro/ bang phyug/ dang dbang phyug chen po dang / tshangs pa dang lha'i bu dpo drug po dang da po dang / nyi ma dang zla ba dang / gnon nu dang gshin rje dang / rgyul
26a4(rgyud): dang lus ngan la sogs gzugs sna tshogs mthong bar 'gyuraro// klu'i rgyal po'i gzugs rnam pa tshogs kyi bar du mthong bar 'gyuraro// ci lta ci ltar sos can rnam 'dus par 'gyur/ 
26a5(rgyud): lha de ltar gzugasu mthong bar 'gyur te/ 'di ni 'jig rten pa'i bzlas brjid bsgrub pa 'bum lag so// 'bum bzlas par 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thos na
26a6(rgyud): nA de bzhin gshegs pa thas cad mngon sum du snang bar 'gyu ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thas cad lung snyan par thob par 'gyur ro// byang chub kyi snying po la thug gi bar du phyir mi ldog par byin
26a7(rgyud): gyis rlabs par 'gyur ro// phyag rgya bcings nis dkyil dkrung bcas te/ sems can thas cad la brtse ba dang 'byung po la byas pa dang snying rje'i sems kyi rang bzhin gyis don yod pa'i zhags pa'i
26b1(rgyud): snying po lan cig bzlas brjod pagyi'o// bzlas brjod bgyis ma thag kho nar lan drug brgya bzhi bcur bzlas bgyis par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dbugs 'byin par mdzad cing
26b2(rgyud): dran pa dang blo gros dang gzi brjod lus la 'jug par bgyid ngo // bzlas brjod bgyis tsam gyi mdo la pha rol du phyin pa drug yongasu rdzogs par 'gyur ro// ri mo'i sku gzugs la yang 'od zer 'byung
26b3(rgyud): bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug yongasu dag pa'i bdag nyid rmi lam du 'thong bar 'gyur ro// mchog thas cad brtsol bar 'gyu ro// de'i las kyi sgrib pa thas cad yongasu byang bar/ 
26b4(rgyud): 'gyu ro// sdig pa dang sgrib pa thas cad yongasu gsal bdang gtugs par 'gyuraro// nang thos cad spangs par 'gyuraro// 'jig rten pa'i dgos pa bsgrub pa rnaMs kyi dam pa thas cad
26b5(rgyud): sgrub par 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas rje su dran bsgom par bgyi'o// 'phags pa don po'i zhags pa'i cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po bam po gsum pa/ thal mo lhan cig sngams te sbyar/ 
26b6(rgyud): rtse mo yad tsam bkug ste/ khar btab la srin lag gnyis phyir kyed cing / gong mo pad ma lta bur bgyis te sngags 'di brjod do// A~M ru ru du ru pad me A mo g+ha sing d+hi b+h+rUM/ phyag rgya 'di ni don ya'i grub lam
26b7(rgyud): rnam grub pa dang ldan pa'i/ 'di ni bcing ba babyis pa yis/ kun rig myur du grub par 'gyur/ myur tu ston pa bcol 'gyur te/ rnyed dga' don yod grub pa'i mched/ mchog kun rab tu stobs par
26b8(rgyud): 'gyur/ 'jig rten 'das pa de bzhin gshegs 'jig rten pa/ sgrib pa thos cad las ni rnam par grol/ bsod nas phung po dag ni rna bar 'phel/ bkra shis sgra ni 'byung bar 'gyur ba'o// lha rnaMs
27a1(rgyud): rtag tu bsrung bar 'gyur/ rdo rje bcings la shin cu ba cing / rtag tu ses ni rtan por bgyi/ 'dzul mo dag ni yid snrums nas/ snying po dag ni rab tu rgyub don yod pa'i dkyil 'khor dang snying
27a2(rgyud): po gsungs pa dang 'dab ma'i dbang phyug gi phyag rgya las dang / don thos cad sgrub pa'i gsang de dag gsungs nas/ de nas don yod pa'i rgyal pos gsungs pa/ oM a mo g+ha hU~M d+ha yang pad me d+ha ra d+ha ra bang
27a3(rgyud): ma d+ha ra ma hA man ta la hr-i ta ya hUM/ stong po phyag rgya 'das ni bcings pa yis/ pad ma 'chang ba'i don yod snying po yi// grub pa de ni yang dag som nyi med/ zas cad tu ni las las rnam par dag/ de ni grub par
27a4(rgyud): 'gyur te som nyi me/ shin tu gsang ba'i phyag rgya bzung / shin cu bsang ba'i gsang sngags zlas/ shin tu dkrus pas gos rtsang gon/ rtsang ma'i sems kyis 'chang bgyid cing / seMs can kun la
27a5(rgyud): rtser gyur nas/ rtag tu bla ma gus par sgom/ rtag tu shin du dang bgyid cing / pad ma'i phyag la dga' bar bgyid/ myur du las grub myur du ni// pad ma 'chang dang sangs rgyas 'thog myur
27a6(rgyud): tu 'jig rten dbang phyug 'thob/ myur du seMs can kun phani ldan// lag pa g.yon pa rkyang tsam gyis/ khar pad ma'i tshul du gzhag la// lag pa sbyar nas 'dzum mo gyen du sgreng / mthe bong yid tsam bkug la/ 
27a7(rgyud): lag pa g.yas parkyang ste/ sor rnas pad ma'i tshul tu gzhag la/ mthe bong yid tsam bkug ste/ gong mo don yod pa'i zhags par bgyi ba ni/ don yod pa zhi ba chen po'i mig sos can tha~Md la byams pa'i
27a8(rgyud): sems dang / snying rje'i bdag nyid can lags te gsang sngags 'di brjod do// AM pa shu pa ti pa ti pa sha d+ha ra sha ta sa ra sh+mi pra ti/ ma Na tri te ka yA/ a ka ri shi na san tsa Ta ni/ b+hu ru b+hu ru/ a mo sha si hI s+yai/ h+yaM
27b1(rgyud): na ni na pa grags pan banan rnas te/ lan tshun tu yang brtag// ngan yong rgyal po bzlas pani bas ma pa mchog tu dag par brtse/ bzlas bcom gyi mngal ni ngan yang nag pa'i phyag rgya mos/ byang
27b2(rgyud): chub zas cad dgugs pa dang // mdol sangs rgyas nyid cu 'gyum gzhan yang rnam pa sna tshogs dag/ ji ltar yid la bses pa bzhin/ mdo la grub pa bla med dang / mdol thams cad 'gugs par
27b3(rgyud): 'gyur// lha dang k+Sha dang gnod sbyin dang // dri za lha min na mkha'// ldeng / mi 'am ci dang lte 'phye dang/ rig sngags 'chang ba lta/ kha'i phyir/ thos cad de'i mad la ni// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas
27b4(rgyud): thas cad dang / de nyid gzigs pas gzigs par 'gyur/ rig sde gas 'chang la phyag bgyi'o phyir/ byang chub seMs dpa' 'du par 'gyur/ mgon po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs mchog/ sbyin
27b5(rgyud): spyi bor phyag 'jog 'gyur// yongasu dag pa bdag nyid kyis/ rang bzhin mod la ston par mdzad/ gang dag mnar med song ba dang / sems can 'tshams med lnga bgyid dang / gang dag 'phag pa skur 'debs dngag
27b6(rgyud): ngag dam chos spong ba dang / phyag rgya mtsho tha~Mng dang 'drir bcug gam/ btsangs pa'i mod la sdig pa kun 'jig 'gyur mod la 'dren pa mthong / phyag rgya bcings pa tsam gyis ni/ dgos pa thas cad 'grub par 'gyur// 
27b7(rgyud): phyag rgya 'di ni mthong tsam dang / rjesu bzlas pa bgyis pa dang // rig sngag 'chang ba mthong ba de// 'phags pa spyan ras gzig dbang gi// mngon sum mthong ba lta bar bya/ tshe rabs rgyud la bskal pa ni/ 
28a1(rgyud): brgya dang stong du bsags pa yi// sdug pa las kyi sgrub pa rnams// phyag rgyas bcings pa mthong tsam gyis// de kun byung 'gyur the tsom med// thal mo lan cig dam sbyar te/ mkhas pa
28a2(rgyud): ma'i tshul du bgyis// sdig 'dzug mo nor bu ltar bgyis te// gong mo yid tsam zhig bkug pa'i/ yid bzhin nor bu rin po che'i rgyal mtshan gyi rtse mo ste// lag pa sbyin por rkyang naso/ spyi bor dbang skur
28a3(rgyud): par brtsol ba'i gsang sngags 'di brjod do/ IM s+t+re yang ta nu ga ta a b+hi shin tsa du/ sarba tre yang tra a b+hi shi ke pad ma ma ni/ su pad me a me go/ sarba ta thA ga te a d+hi ShI te hUM/ 'dis dbang skur pa tsam
28a4(rgyud): gyis rig sngags 'chang la// de bzhin gsheg pa thams cadakyis dbang skur bar 'gyuraro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzig/ dbang phyug gi dbang skur bar 'gyur// rig sngags 'chang gi
28a5(rgyud): rgyal po chen por 'gyur ro// rig sngags 'chang thas cad 'gyu/ par 'gyur ro// nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa thas cad rnam par dag/ par 'gyuraro// 'jig rten thos cad kyi rtse bo gcig pa'i gan su 'gyur
28a6(rgyud): spyi bo phyug rdo rje pad ma bcing rtag tu sor mo rtse mo rkyang // 'dzub mo lcags kyu'i tshul du bgyi/ rang gi dong gi khro gnyis bzhin/ khro bo'i rgyal po phyag rgya che/ las kun grub par bgyid pa yi/ thas cad grub
28a7(rgyud): dpying phyag rgya ste/ kun grub pad ma'i gsang sngags can// 'di 'dra sgrub pa kun gyi mchog/ oM khro d+ha ra tsa d+ha ma hA a mo g+ha ha na ha na/ sarba duSh+TA na hrI/ phyag rgya 'di ni dran tsam gyis// mthu chen po'i gsang
28a8(rgyud): sngags kyis/ 'dug pa kun ni rnam par 'jig/ ri rab kyang ni snyim par byed/ phyag rgya bcings pa tsam gyis ni/ sdig pa thas cad 'jig par bgyid// sos can 'dug pa 'dug pa'i k+Sha// 'gag dang log
28b1(rgyud): len 'drug dus/ de gapas cang ni bar pa/ phyag rtsub cings pa tsam gyis ni/ bas cad dbyung dra gyu nas mam/ lU dang mi dang dge sbyong dang / bram de rgyal rigs gang lags pa/ tham cang pa
28b2(rgyud): tu byung nas myi mchis par 'gyur bar the tsam maung rgyud ni rtag du mnyam gzhag la// mtho mnyam du bte gnas ni// gung mo yis ni grong mo nyid/ yid tsam bkug nas sbeng bar bgyi// 'dun
28b3(rgyud): bde ma chen mo yis// lha mo sgrol ma'i phyag rgya ste/ grub pa bla na med pa yaM/ thas cad kyi ni dam pa lags/ thal mo pad ma'i tshul du sbyar/ mthe bong gnyis ni rkyang bgyis la/ mthe'u chung yad tsam
28b4(rgyud): bkug pa ni/ kar shar chen mo phyag rgya ste/ de ni kun grub bla/ na med/ rdo rje'i tshul du thal sbyar dam bcing shing / shes ra bo can gyis g.yas pa'i lag sgyur la/ khro gnyer bzhin de bzhin
28b5(rgyud): khro bo dang / phyag rgya chen po kun 'od rab tu sbyin// lag gnyis kyi thal sbyar nas/ gsang ba de rkyang gung mo bkug nas su/ mthe cung rkyang nas lcags kyu pad ma yi// tshul du snying kha'i gzhag
28b6(rgyud): pad par bya/ phyag rgya 'di ni phyag rgya che/ phyag rgya 'di ni bcings pa yis// zhal sbyar dkyil 'khor kun nas lha dag dang / thas cad 'tshogs shing 'dra ba dang / kun gyis bsrung bgyid so ma nyi med// phyag rgya
28b7(rgyud): 'di nyid bshig nas lhag pa ni// thal sbyar pad ma'i tshul du byA/ snying khar gzhag nas gnod sbyin po nya ma'i// 'di ni phyag rgya lag pas legs par bsgrags// dang po rdo rje khu tshur legs bcings pa/ 
28b8(rgyud): gung mo lhag ma skum zhing mthe bong gzhag/ pad ma'i tshul du bzhin dran sgrol 'dud kyi/ grub pa kun gyi bla med phyag rgya'ang / sdig pa thos cang 'jig cing nyon mongs kun/ nang kun nye bar ni bar som nyi ma
29a1(rgyud): don byung kun sgrub pa'i rna med / chogan ba sgo mas cad ra bcu phyug/ lag pa gnyis ni mnam gnag ste/ rdorje rnal ru pa ma bcing / 'drub mo bkug pa brgyas ni/ mthe bang yang
29a2(rgyud): ni dgug par bgyi/ 'di na ta mgrin phyag rgya ste/ zlum mo klong gi khalta bu/ rdo rje za ba nyid kyis gsungs 'dzi na las kun bgyid pa po// grub pa kun gyi bla na med/ phyag rgya 'di ni 'dzub mo'i mthe
29a3(rgyud): bong gnyis// sngags sgrog lhag ma skams na pad ma'i tshul/ snyid kha gan su gzhag par mgrin sngon gyi// 'di ni dgos med las kyi phyag rgya lags/ la gnyis pad ma'i khu tshur te/ g.yas g.yon
29a4(rgyud): dro ni gzhag gnas kun nas zhi ba'i gzhan du gzhag/ dbyas pa'i phyag gnyis bgyid pa ni/ zhal ni bcu gcig phyag/ rgyu ste/ de bzhin kun gyis mi thub pa'o// mthe bong mnyam par
29a5(rgyud): mnyam bgyis pa/ ser mo rtse mo snum pa dang / 'dzub mo da zhes ni pad ma'i tshul/ rig pa 'ing dang phyag phyag rgya lags phyag rgya 'di nyid dbus su mi 'khor lo tshul du 'dzub mo skum/ g.yan
29a6(rgyud): brkyang dbang chen gyi/ phyag rgya byung ba zas cad 'joms/ lhag song ma chubagyis nas naM/ lag pa gnyis parkyang nas no// snyid khar gnag pa'i phyag rgya ste/ 'dzi ni rgyun drug shin rje legs lag pa g.yon
29a7(rgyud): rkyang nas su/ sor mo sbreng ba'i thong to dgug/ g.yas ba steng khar gzhag nas/ mthe bong dang ni mthe chung dgug/ lhag ma nas ni rkyang bgyis te/ phyag rgya 'dzi ni lha'i phyag rgya ste/ klu kun dgug pa'i mchog
29a8(rgyud): lag so// lag pa gnyis ni snga mas bgyis la// sor mo phyin ci log tu sbrel/ g.yas pa dang ni g.yon pa dag/ snying gi gnasu gzhag bgyis ste/ phyag rgya 'di ni lus ngan gyi/ gnod sbyin thas cad
29b1(rgyud): skrag par bgyid/ lag pa g.yas pa spyi bor yab mthe bong 'dzub mo dgug 'phyis pa/ lag pa g.yon brkyang nas/ 'dzub mo byin du sbreng ba ni/ 'di ni tshangs pa'i phyag rgya ste/ zas cad du ni las

30b5(rgyud): tshe ring bar 'gyu ro// nad thas cad las thar par 'gyu ro// skyon gyi dri ma dang ser sna dang / 'phra dog thas cad dang bral bar 'gyu ro// legs pa ra dAn cing lus shin du yongasu dag pa 'gyur/

30b7(rgyud): rten gyi khas bde bar can du song shig/ ces shin tu drin pa nye bar gzhag nas/ dus byed par 'gyu ro// dmyal ba'i sgo thos cad bcad par 'gyu ro// ngan song gi sgo thas cad las yongasu grol bar 'gyuraro// 
30b8(rgyud): 'di nas ma 'ongs pa mang du skye bar 'gyur// skye ba rtag tu skye ba dran par 'gyuraro// zas cad du pad ma la rdzus te skye bar 'gyur ro// byang chub kyi snying po la thug gi bar du/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sangs
