110a3(rgyud): spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song ste phyin nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag la grub pa don yod pa'i snying po rigs sngags kyi rgyal po'i snying po gang gis
110a4(rgyud): gas pa tsam gyis don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po myur tu rab tu 'grub cing / dran pa tsam gyis 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug/ lha'i lus ston pa'i 'gyur ba/ dngos grub dang mchog thams cad sbyin par 'gyur ba
110a5(rgyud): mchis te/ bcom ldan 'das de bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan ras gzigs 'khor gyi dkyil 'di nang du yongs su bsgrag par bgyi'o// na mo rang na tra ya yA/ na mo a mi da pa ya/ ta thA gA ta yA/ na mo ar+ya ba lo
110a6(rgyud): ki ti shA ra yA/ bod de sang tA yA/ matA sad tA yA/ ma hA ka ru ni ka yA/ tad+ya thA/ AM pad me pad me/ pad ma da ra bi bu shi te tse/ tsi ra tsa ra/ pra ma be sha da ra/ bi tse ta me'u le da ra/ ma ni ka na badz+ra be du ra lang kri ta sha ri ra/ 
110a7(rgyud): taM ra ta ra/ da ra ya ba gra ban/ bA gA be tri ba ri ni// du ru du ru/ a mo ga ba sha ha ste/ ba ra ba ra/ da ya kaM sa man te/ A ba lo ki ti/ ma ha bod de/ sad tA yA/ ba ra dA/ pad ma sa na/ pad ma ge'u ra badz+ra la dzA la
110a8(rgyud): sarba ta thA g+hA ta/ A bi shi ka/ a byi shi gA te/ ma hA kra ru ni ka/ ba la ba la/ ma hA ba ga da ra/ bi kri ta ya na dang / sta ka ra la ma hA da tse/ da ra de ra/ bil+yA tsa na pa ra ta/ mahA ka ru na ka/ ma hA ba shu ba ta be sha dar/ sa ra sar
110b1(rgyud): pra pa ra su n+ya sa ma pa ra/ su ga tad t+ya na sa mi ti/ sra man ta A ba lo ki te/ i sha ra ma ma hA shwa ra/ du sta da ma ke reru tra pra la dam ka/ khro dar tsa ma hA be ge dar rta sa ma sa ma/ ma hA sA ma pra ba ta tsan tra se'u ra
110b2(rgyud): a ti ra ka pra pam la maM la ta sarba ma la bi sha da kA/ sarba ri shi ka na san ta ti ma hA ma ti sha ra ru sa ra ra/ a mi da ba dzA ni la ki ta dza ta/ ta kri ni tsan ta lang kri ta shi ra/ ma tha ma thA sarba ra kA ra k+Sha/ sa pu ta ga na bAn dza kre/ 
110b3(rgyud): ta ra ta raHka na sa ma lang kri tA nA karma ma la/ sarba ba gi na bi na sha na ka ra ba ra me tra tsing tra/ mang+ka ka ru ni kra/ ba ra ba ra/ pa ri bu rna man da la/ se'u mya mu kha shad pa ri ma ta su ra ke/ mi li mi li/ e ne ya tsarman+di
110b4(rgyud): ba sa sa na/ byA gra narmo data ta rI mi// da ra da ra/ sarba ta thA ga tA/ ma sa lo kri tin+de dra ri/ tri shul dai rarA badz+ri dz+wa la da ra/ A mo go ba sha hA ha sti/ ya mA sa ru ne/ ku be ra du ne/ ne gren dra rus dA ra bi ma la tra
110b5(rgyud): shud dAHdwe dwaudas pa pa pa sra sha ma ka/ sarba a ba ra na bi shod da ka/ sa ra ki la bi sha na sha ke/ tre log d+ya be shad ka ra rAHsarba sad tA bi sha ta ka/ bod de sad tA ba ra/ sarba ta thA gA ta U te s+t+rI ta/ AM pad ma bi pu shi
110b6(rgyud): tadr-i shwad d+heHd+hi ri d+hi rIta A ba lo ki ya mnaHsa ma sa ma/ sarba karma ma me sa d+h+ya/ a me ba shrA hri da yA/ sid de gud t+ye ni pa ni ba ra da h+ni phaT/ na mo stu te swA hA/ grub pa don yod pa'i rigs sngags kyi rgyal po
110b7(rgyud): 'di bshad pa zag tu 'byung po'i tshigs dang / gnod pa sbyin dang / srin po drang bgogs dang / lo ga 'dren thams cad khaM srub tu 'gyel tu gcig tu 'bar 'bar bar 'gyur cing / gnas kyang 'bar 'gyur ba dang
110b8(rgyud): de nas gnod basbyin gyi sde dpon chen po phyag na rdo rje dag pos/ ba bskulangs te skrag pur 'gyur te/ lha'i tshogs thams cad dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang khyab 'jug dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / 
101'a1(rgyud): d+h+we rgyal po chen po bzhi dang / bsgrag par 'gyur ba'i lha dang / lha ma yin dang / drang srong sA gong ba thams cad dang / rgya mtsho na gnas pa'i klu'i rgyal po thams cad dang / chu bran
101'a2(rgyud): thams cad dang / lha dang klu gang dgra chun gnas pa thams cad dang / rgya mtsho chen po'i lha dang / lha gang dag lang ga'i grong khyer gnas pa thams cad dang / rigs sngags 'chang gis 'khor lo sgyur ba thams
101'a3(rgyud): cad dang / gang dag gnas gtsang mi'i rigs kyi lha rnams dang / nam mkha'i lha thams cad 'khrug par 'gyur nas/ nam mkha' las babs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las dang / byang chub seMs
101'a4(rgyud): dpa' 'phags pa spyan+da ras gzigs dbang phyag de la yang mchod pa'i 'phyir/ lha'i me tog rnam pa sna tshogs pa/ prad/ ma dang / ku mu ta dang / ud pa la dang / pun+da dari ka dang / man dAr ba
101'a5(rgyud): dang / man da ra ba chen po'i char dang / lha'i rkyen dang / lbab lhub kyi char bu sau mo nub pa tsam ri bo pe ta lar phi ba ste/ lha'i sil snyan dang / k+ShuM dbyangs len cing / ha ha tsa tse dang gzha'i sgra btod nas/ bcom
101'a6(rgyud): ldan 'das 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis/ sems can thams cad kyi don du rigs sngags chen mo bshad do zhes ched do brjod pa chen po 'di chen du brjod do// de nas gnod sbyin gyi ste dpon chen po lag na rdo rje/ 
101'a7(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gang na ba der song ste/ lan gsum skor ba byas nas mchod pa'i phyir mu tig gi do shal brgya stong ri ba phul te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
101'a8(rgyud): rigs snga chen po'i cho ga zhib mo thams cad kyi mchog bshad do/ don yod pa'i rgyal po rigs pa chen po'i snying po mgon po thub pa chen po bshad du gsol bcom ldan 'das cho ga bzhi mo grub pa don yod pa'i rgyal po grub pa'i
101'b1(rgyud): mchog las thams cad 'grub par bshad du gsol/ de nas de'i 'og tu 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gis/ don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po'i cho ga zhib mo grub pa don yod pa'i rigs sngags kyi rgyal po ras kyi
101'b2(rgyud): sku gzugs bsgrub pa'i mchog cho ga dang / yo byad du bcas pa bshad pa/ ras grub bzhi pa kun nas cha legs par byed pa/ kha tshar ma bcud pa/ sgra med pa/ ri mo mkhan rtsangs khrus byas gos kyang ma bgos la gso sbyong
101'b3(rgyud): dang ldan par byas pas/ tshen lhag ma ma yin pa/ snod gsar par gzhag par bri bar bya ste/ dbus su 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ral pa'i tshor tshugs kyi sa bzhug shing rgyal 'od dpag med kyis
101'b4(rgyud): dbu brgyan po/ thor tshugs kyi g.yus su zla/ tshes kyis brgyan pa/ ri dgas e na ya'i lpags pa gon pa/ phyugs bdag gi cha/ lugs 'tshang ba/ rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ dbu gsum spyan gsum
101'b5(rgyud): phyag bzhi/ ri'i steng na pad ma'i steng na bzhugs pa/ zhal dbus ma zhig pa'i gzhin 'dzum pa// zhal g.yas pa'i gajigs su rung ba// 'khro gnyer can thor tshugs 'od dpag med kyis rkyen pa// dbu zla ches rgyan da
101'b6(rgyud): zhol grayon pa 'jigs su rung ba/ bzhin sgyur cing mche ba martsigs pa/ rgyu lu phra 'od dpag med dbus la bzhugs pa/ phyag cig na padad+ma ma thogs/ gnyis pa na rtse gsum thogs gsum pa na don yod pa'i zhwan/ 
101'b7(rgyud): bsku'i phyed na 'dzin pa/ bcom ldan 'das zhil khro gnyer can sman gtod par bya zhing zhi bar bugs 'byin pa'i phyag tu ba ste/ 'od 'od ma gang ba khor yug tu 'bar ba dang ldan par bya'o// g.yas phyogs su lha mo sgrol ma/ mdzes
101'b8(rgyud): bge dang bcas shing lus btud pa/ mchod sprin gyi phyag rgya lo mig gtad par bya'o// g.yom du pad ma'i rigs mdzes ma bag dang bcas pa/ gsang sngags kyi tshul dang rjes su 'thun zhing / don yod pa'i zhags pa la
102'a1(rgyud): mig gtong bar bya'o// mo sgrol ma'i bar du gnod sbyin ma ral pa gcig ma pa'o// ba'i pad ma'i rigs mdzes ma'i bar du khro gnyer ba'o// phyogs gnyis par lta bar lha mo dkar mo phyag na pad ma thogs
102'a2(rgyud): pa bya'o// pad ma'i rigs mdzes ma'i 'og tu pho nya mo gsang sngags kyi rjes su bar ba'o// ral pa gcig ma'i 'og tu lha mo chen mo 'jigs byengs pa'o// 'og tu gnas rtsang ma'i rigs kyis lha'i bu dang / brgya byin dang / 
102'a3(rgyud): tshangs pa dang / khab 'jug dang dbang phyug son po me tog sna tshogs thogs te// bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa byed par bya'o// 'og tu ril po chen po bzhi pa'o// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyog gi 'og tu
102'a4(rgyud): 'phags pa phyag ni rdo rje 'jig su rung ba ga rgyangs can/ khro bo don yod pa'i rgyal po ngasmra bar bya'o// ras kyi sgo gzugs 'di mthong ba tsan dgyes// 'phag sla rus gzigs dbang phyug ri bo bo ti li na gzhal med
102'a5(rgyud): khang dang bcas pa mngon sum du mthong bar rlig par bya'o// 'phags pa don yod pa'i zhags pa'i cho ga zhib me'i rgyal po// // bam po bcu pa// / mthong ba tsam gyis
102'a6(rgyud): sems can dmyal ba chen po brgyad las thar bar 'gyur ro// 'jigs pa chen po brgyad las yongs su grol bar 'gyur ro// 'tshams med pa lnga byed pa yang yongs su thar bar 'gyur ro// dam pa'i chos spong ba dang / 
102'a7(rgyud): sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad spong bas mthong ba tsam gyis mdo las/ rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// mnar med pa la gzhol ba'i 'thar thug par yang yongs su grol bar 'gyur ro// tshangs pa chen po'i bsod nam/ 
102'a8(rgyud): brgya stong gi dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed par 'gyur ro// 'jig rten thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba mchog thob par 'gyur ro/ 'chi ba'i dus na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug mngon sum du ston par 'gyur zhing / dbugs 'byin
102'b1(rgyud): bar 'gyur sbyin 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du skye bar 'gyur// grib pa thams cad dang bral nas/ tshe rabs brgya stong phrag sbyar rjesu dran par 'gyur/ byang chub kyi snying po mthar thug par du skye ba 'di tha ma yin te/ 
102'b2(rgyud): 'di mthong ba tsam gyis bsod nams phung po dang ldan par 'gyur na/ lhag par mang du byed par 'gyur ba lta ci smos te/ de ni phyir mi ldog par 'gyur/ bla na med pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par 'gyur ro// 
102'b3(rgyud): gal te rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo 'am/ dge slong dum dge slong ma 'am/ dge slong snyen nam// dge snyen mo nam/ rgyal po 'am blon po dang / dartson mo 'khor dang bcas pa 'am// btsun mo dam pa gang
102'b4(rgyud): la la zhig gis ras kyi sku gzugs bsgrub par byed pa de'i spyan sngar/ dge don yod zhags pa'i snying po dran par byed cing / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug de yang mchod pa par byed na/ des
102'b5(rgyud): na khyod kyis 'di lngar rig par bya ste/ de na yod pa'i zhag pa'i snying po stong phrag brgya 'gyur du bzlas shing / bzlas brjod kyi cho ga chen po byas pa yin no/ gang zhig khro bo don yod pa'i
102'b6(rgyud): zhags pa bcom ldan 'das kyi skyon sngar mi smra bar lan gsum bzlas brjod bgyis te/ chus dbang skur ba des na khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad kyis bdag
102'b7(rgyud): byang chub kyi snying po la mthar thug gi ber ta dbang skur bar 'gyur snyam du de ltar shes rab par bya'o// gang gis de ni yod par 'grub pa'i cho ga zhib mo'o gzugs/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug
102'b8(rgyud): gi res kyi sku gzugs kyi spyan sngar mngon sum tu thal mo sbyar te 'dug nas lAn bdun bzlas te bskor ba lan bdun byas te/ chu'i mchod yon dang lha bshos dang / bdug spos dang me tog phul la nas bag
103'a1(rgyud): 'tshal lo zhes smras na/ des na khyod kyis 'di ltar shes par byas te/ gsungs thams cad so sor lan stong phrag brgyar bzlas par 'gyur zhing / don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po rnam grangs
103'a2(rgyud): ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi rnam grangs chen po 'di lan stong phrag brgya bzlas par 'gyur ro// don yod pa'i zhags pa'i phyag rgyabs la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi zhal du mig gtad de/ lag pa
103'a3(rgyud): g.yas g.yon gnyis snying khar bzhag pa'i tshul 'dris phyag rgya re re nas lan stong phrag brgya byas par 'gyuraro/ bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu'om/ rigs kyi bu mo 'am/ rige slong ngam dge slong ma'am/ rgyal/ 
103'a4(rgyud): po'am rgyal mo'am btsun mo dam pa gang la la zhig/ 'phag pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po 'di brgya stong phrag khri bzlas rjod bya bar 'dod pa dang / don yod pa/ 
103'a5(rgyud): zhags pa'i phyag rgya 'di lan stong phrag khrir bya bar 'dod pa dang / rnam par grol ba'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dag gi cho ga zhib mo 'di ldan stong phrag khri bzla bar 'dod pa dang / don yod pa'i phyag rgya 'di lan stong phrag khrir bya
103'a6(rgyud): bar 'dod pa des/ ras kyi sku gzugs la mtshon par byas te/ ras kyi sku mngon du bzhag nas rtsang zhing bde ba'i gnas sam/ 'chag sa 'am dgon pa'i gnas sam/ phug gam rI'i rtse mo'am/ rtsug lag khang
103'a7(rgyud): ngam/ khang bsngar rtsang ma sgra dang byi dror byas te/ ba ser mo'i lci ba legs par mnyes te/ ba las byung ba lnga dang sres te skus la/ spos sna tshogs kyi byug pa byas nas/ ras kyi sku gzugs kyi spyan sngar
103'a8(rgyud): tsan dan dkar po'i dkyil 'khor byas te/ gu re gum gyis khru do ba'i tshad tsam bris la/ bla ci rtsi dang ga bur gyis mchod pa bya'o// dri chab kyi bum pa dri rnam pa sna tshogs bkang ste/ ras kyis mgul bcings la dkyil 'khon
103'b1(rgyud): dbus su bzhag par bya/ me tog dang bdug spos kyi snod dri zhim po dang / me tog phreng ba nyi shu rtsa cig bzhag par bya'o// dri chab kyis bkang ba brgyad phyogs bzhir bzhag par bya'o// 'o mas bkang ba'i snod brkyang zhag
103'b2(rgyud): par bya'o// stegs bu'i steng du 'o mas bkang ba'i snod bzhag par bya/ 'o dug dang sbyar dug dang khan da khan bya dang / 'bras tshan lan pan dang / bu ram dang ka ra dang / zhun mar gyis bkang ba'i snod bzhag par bya'o// 
103'b3(rgyud): a ka ru nag po dang tsan dan dkar po dang / ga bur dang kun du tu dang / shi ri pa sa ka dang / chung sed rnas dang snod du bzhag nas/ A ru yi yam shing gi sbyin sreg bya/ me tog sna tshogs kyis brgyan par bya/ mar gyi mar
103'b4(rgyud): me sna tsho gsum bcu rtsa bdun bltam par bya'o// de nas rigasngags 'chang rtsang mas dgas shing khrus legs par byas pas/ tshes bcu/ bzhi nas bco lnga'i bar du 'phags pa spyan ras zigs dbang chug
103'b5(rgyud): kyi ras kyi sku gzugs la mchod pa bya'o// de'i 'og tu rig sngags kyis khro bo'i rgyal po lan bdun zlas te/ dri chab kyis dbang skur bar bya'o/ do ni yod pa'i zhags pa'i zhags pa'i phyag rgya la na nyi shu rtsa cig bya/ 
103'b6(rgyud): de nas mi smra bar dkyil mo drung du 'dug ste zlas rjod kyi phyag rgya bcings la/ don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po lan brgya rtsa brkyad zlas par bya'o// de nas de'i 'og tu don yod grub pa'i rig sngags kyi rgyal po stong rtsa brkyad zlas
103'b7(rgyud): par bya/ de nas ras kyi sku gzugs la 'od zer bdun byung nas/ kun nas snang bar byas te lan gsum skor ba byas te/ 'phags pa spyan ras zigs dbang phyug spyan drang zhugs par 'gyur/ zhugs pa tsam gyi mong
103'b8(rgyud): la sa cher g.yos par 'gyur zhing / rig sngags 'chang yang snying dga' zhing ba sku ldang bar 'gyur/ mdog mdangs yongasu dag par 'gyur/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi mchod sbyin gyi phyag
104'a1(rgyud): rgyu sor mo las/ lha'i chu 'dzag par 'gyur/ zhabs gnyis las 'o ma 'dzag par 'gyur/ don yod pa'i zhabs pa'i rgyu phyag rgya 'bar bar 'gyur/ phyag na pa'i lo ma g.yo bar
104'a2(rgyud): 'gyur/ rtse gsum g.yo bar 'gyur// zhing / legs so zhes bya ba'i sgra 'byung bar 'gyur te// rigs kyi bu legs so legs so/ khyod kyis don yod pa'i zhabs pa'i snying por grub par gyis/ las thams
104'a3(rgyud): cad byos shig/ khyod kyis don yod grub pa'i cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po dam pa grub pa zhes nas/ de nas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gzugs snyan par mdzad do/ 'dod pa thams cad kyi
104'a4(rgyud): mchog sbyin par mdzad do/ 'di ni grub pa'i mchog bla na med pa ste/ ma bsgrubs par las byed pa'o// de nas dbang du bya bar 'dod na/ me tog pad ma la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas la/ 'phags pa spyan ras
104'a5(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug la phul te/ gang ming nas brjod de/ dbang du 'gyur ro// sna'i me tog la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas te// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la phul la/ yang lan bdun
104'a6(rgyud): bzlas nas/ me tog snyim pa blangs te/ gang la byin pa de dbang du 'gyur ro/ ga don thams cad las yongs su grol bar 'gyur ro// nad kyis thebs pa la byin na/ nad thams cad las grol bar 'gyur// 
104'a7(rgyud): rgyal po'i sgor gtor na rgyal po'i btsun mo'i 'khor dang / bcas pa dbang du 'gyur ro/ mi re sregs pa'i stengs su tor nas/ sems can de sems can dmyal ba las grol bar 'gyur ro/ ma nar med pa gnas
104'a8(rgyud): pa'i sems can dmyal ba rnams la rtor na/ skad cig de las yongs su grol bar 'gyur ro// nyal ba'i sngas su gzhag nas ma rmi lam chen po mthong bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug sku stonas par
104'b1(rgyud): mdzad cing yid du 'ong ba thams cad gsung bar 'gyur ro// skyes pa 'am bud med gang gi steng du gtor ba de dbang du 'gyur zhing grib ma bzhin 'brang bar 'gyur ro/ rgyal po'i stengadu rtor na bran bzhin du 'gyur ro// lha'i
104'b2(rgyud): gzugs brnyan gyi steng du gzhag na 'gugs par 'gyur ro/ las thams cad byed par 'gyur ro/ mig sman la bsgrub par 'dod pas/ ras kyi sku gzugs kyi spyan sngar mig sman ldong ros la lan stong rtsa brgyad
104'b3(rgyud): bzlas te/ grub pa'i rtags bcu ston par 'gyur te/ 'bar ba dang / dbugs 'byung ba dang / tud pa 'byung bar 'gyur te/ des mig la skus te snang bar 'gyur te/ gter thams mthong bar 'gyur ro// 
104'b4(rgyud): gnod sbyin gyi gnas thams cad mthong bar 'gyur ro/ bral bar thig le byas na/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug thams cad du 'jug par 'gyur ro/ sgo thams cad dang / 'khrul 'khor thams cad dbye bar 'gyur/ 
104'b5(rgyud): yan lag dang nying lag la skus na nam mkha' la 'khor bar 'gyur ro// dbye bor thig le byas na/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzig dbang phyug la gyis mchod sbyin par 'gyur ro// mig la byugs na/ khyab
104'b6(rgyud): 'jug dang dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa lha thams cad rtag tu phyi bzhin 'brang bar 'gyur zhing / dgos pa thams cad 'grub par byed do// mtshan mo mig la smras na/ nyin bzhin tu mthong bar 'gyur zhing / gter thams
104'b7(rgyud): cad 'byung bar 'gyur te/ khas phul nas dor bar bya'o// rang gyi lus la byugs na stong 'tsho'i bar du go cha dgos pa'i lus su 'gyur ro/ gnod sbyin dang srin po la spogs pas mi mthong bar 'gyur zhing / las thams cad byed par
104'b8(rgyud): 'gyur ro// tshe skal pa stong thub par 'gyur ro// bza' ba dang khir sgru ba byas na/ nag po chen po'i gzugs mthong bar 'gyur zhing / lha thams cad kyis gzugs stong par 'gyur nas/ tshangs pa dang khyab 'jug dang dbang
105'a1(rgyud): phyag chen po'i gzugs dang / gzugs sna tshogs yongs su ston par 'gyur ro// zla ba dang nyi ma ston par 'gyur ro// ldong ros dang 'gyi wang dang / se'u bi rig dang / gur gum dang / ku ku pa la don yod par
105'a2(rgyud): grub pa khri bzlas/ don yod par zhags pa'i snying po stong rtsa brgyad bzlas/ khro bo'i rgyal po brgya rtsa brgyad byas te thams cad du mi smra bar byas shing / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gyi spyan spang btags la ras kyi sku
105'a3(rgyud): gzugs la mngon par phyogs te/ rtsang mas mos rtsang ma gos la/ chos bcwo pa nya la zhag cig snang ba byas nas phye ma zhib tu btags te/ yang don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po dang / khro bo'i rgyal po dang / don yod pa'i grub pa'i
105'a4(rgyud): rigs sngags kyi rgyal po brgyad bzlas brjod byas la kha de'i 'og tu 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gyi phyag tu gzhag ste/ mchod pa chen po byas nas ras kyi sku gzugs la mchod pa byas la nyin zhig cig sbyang ba
105'a5(rgyud): byas te bzlas brjod kyi phyag rgya byas la/ khro bo'i lan bdun bzlas te/ de'i 'og tu mig la skus na/ don yod pa'i grub pa'i gzungs bzlas pa byas na/ skus pa tsam gyis 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug
105'a6(rgyud): ri bo po ta la dang bcas gzhal med khang dang bcas/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs gzhal med khang dang bcas pa/ ri bo pe ta la gnas pa mthong bar 'gyur ro// bde ba can gyi 'jig rten gyi khams mthong zhing
105'a7(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med chos 'chad pa mthong bar 'gyur ro// chos bshad pa de yang thob par 'gyur ro// phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs dang bcas/ nyan thos kyi tshogs dang / 
105'a8(rgyud): bcas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhal med khang bcas pa mthong bar 'gyur zhing / chos bshad pa'i gsung gyi sgra zos par 'gyur ro/ 'di ltar rigs ngan gyi rigs su skyes pa dang / mnar med par gzhol ba dang
105'b1(rgyud): 'tshams med pa lnga byas pa gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis rlabs pa dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi thugs rjes dgongs par 'gyur zhing / rmi la
105'b2(rgyud): du ston par mdzad do// sdig pa dang / sgrib pa thams cad rnam par dag par sbyong bar 'gyur/ mchog thams cad sbyin par 'gyur ro// don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po dngos grub sbyin par 'gyur/ lha'i lo stong tshe
105'b3(rgyud): bar 'gyur zhing lha'i bde ba nyams su myong bar 'gyur/ nad kyis thebs pa thams cad la mig sman 'di smras na/ nang thams cad zhi bar 'gyur zhing / rims nad zhi bar 'gyur ro// dag thams cad la skus pa tsam gyis
105'b4(rgyud): tug med par 'gyu ro// 'jigs pa thams cad la mig la skus na/ mi mthong bar 'gyur/ phyir dgol ba dang dgra dang / g.yo can/ dang chom po dang / rkun po thams cad kyis mi mthong bar 'gyur/ 
105'b5(rgyud): mtshon gyi 'jigs par mi 'gyur ro/ 'thab pa dang rtsod pa dang / khrag 'khrug pa la mig la skus na/ thams cad du rgyal zhing lan thebs par 'gyur ro// g.yul po thams can du mig la skus na/ 
105'b6(rgyud): g.yul 'gyed pa la rgyal bar 'gyur zhing / dpung gi tshogs las rgyal bar 'gyur ro// rgyal po'i pho brang du 'gro ba'i tshe mig la smras na/ rgyal po'i btsun mo 'khor dang bcas pa dbang du 'gyur ro// mi smra bar
105'b7(rgyud): grong khyer du song na/ skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang bu mo grong khyer du gnas so// mchog thams cad dbang du 'gyur ro/ mig g.yas pa la skyes na/ rigs ba ni'i 'jig rten gang mthong ba dris
105'b8(rgyud): thams cad du 'gyur ro/ mig g.yon kha la skus na/ rigs ngan thams cad du 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gyi phyag g.yas pa nas/ gzung ste/ don yod pa'i grub pa'i rigs
106'a1(rgyud): sngags kyi rgyal po lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brjod byas te 'phags pa spyan sre gzigs dbang phyug la mchod pa byas na/ de nas don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po dang / khro bo'i rgyal po dang
106'a2(rgyud): gsungs thams cad so sor lan stong phrag brgya bzlas par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bye ba stong phrag bcu'i drung du dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed par 'gyur/ 
106'a3(rgyud): thams cad kyi ming bzung bar 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa stong mnyes pa byas par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs/ pa stong phrag drug bcu rtsa bzhi mngon sum tu mthong ba 'gyur/ 'jig rten pa'i don thams cad
106'a4(rgyud): 'grub par 'gyur/ sngon gyi sgrib pas mnar med pa'i gnas su 'gro ba yongs su dag par 'gyur/ nams kyang ngan song du 'gro bar 'gyur ro// tshe rabs tshe rabs su skye ba dran par 'gyur/ lha thams
106'a5(rgyud): cad kyang mchog sbyin par 'gyur zhing / rtag tu bsrung pa dang skyab pa dang / sba bar byed par 'gyur ro// phyag g.yon pa gnan te lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas brtsod byas na/ bzlas pa tsam gyi
106'a6(rgyud): mod la lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / srin po la sogs par 'gyur zhing / thams cad dbang du 'gyur bar gnas so// gang gi tshe dgos par 'gyur ba de'i tshe/ don yod par grub pa de'i rigs sngags kyi
106'a7(rgyud): rgyal po lan bdun bzlas pa byas na/ lha dang klu la sogs pa thams cad kyang las thams cad byed cing rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par phyi bzhin 'brang bar 'gyur ro// lte ba'i gnas tu gnan te/ bzlas na klu la sogs pa
106'a8(rgyud): thams cad char gyi rgyun 'bebs par 'gyuraro/ 'jam pa'i gling mtha' dag tshim pa byed par 'gyur ro snyam du lan brgyad rtsa brgyad bzlas na/ gang dang gang du song ba der skyes pa dang bud med dang / rgyal po dang blon
106'b1(rgyud): po dgra dge slong ngam/ bram ze 'am/ dge snyen nam/ dge sen ma la gang la bsams pa dang / gang bcol ba dang / gang smras pa'i las de thams cad grub par 'gyur ro// dbugs nas bzung ste// bzlas na/ tshangs
106'b2(rgyud): pa 'jig sa rten gyi khams kyi bar du byas par 'gyur te/ thams cad la dbang skur zhing sgo ba bzhin byed par 'gyur ro// thog mar bzlas brjod stong rtsa brgyad byas nas bzlas par bya'o// zhabs gnyis gnan te stong phrag
106'b3(rgyud): bcu bzlas pa byas na sa'i 'og yan chad dbang du byas par 'gyur zhing las thams cad byed par 'gyur te/ mngag gzhug thams cad byed par 'gyur ro/ pad ma la stong rtsa brgyad bzlas nas/ pad ma'i mtshe'u ra bob na/ 
106'b4(rgyud): pad ma'i zad mi shes par 'byung zhing / pad ma dus thams cad par 'gyur ro// ud pa dang la la lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas nas/ ud pa la/ la'i mtshe'ur bor na/ ud pal la sngon po zad mi shes pa
106'b5(rgyud): 'byung 'gyur zhing / nams kyang nyams par mi 'gyur te/ dus thams cad tu me tog 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du snga ma'i me tog dang / gnangs shi ka dang / yu ti ka dang / na ma li ka'i me tog
106'b6(rgyud): rnams kyang // dus thams cad du me tog 'byung bar 'gyur zhing / zad mi shes par 'gyur ro 'bras bu dang me tog la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas te// skyed mos tshal lam ka nags tshal gyi nang du gtor na me tog
106'b7(rgyud): dang 'bras bu zad mi shing tus thams cad par 'gyur ro// dpal chen po bkug par 'dod pas/ sra tshil las dpal chen po'i dkyil 'khor mo dkrung byed du 'dug la rgyan thams cad pas brgyan pa/ lus 'dud
106'b8(rgyud): bya lag na pad ma thogs pa brang rgyas pa byas la 'bras bu dang me tog 'gram par bya zhing / ga pur dang bla rtsi dang / tsan dan dkar pos mchod pa byas la/ ras kyi sku gzugs kyi sman ra sngar gzhag par bya zhing / 
107'a1(rgyud): 8// sngar tsan dan dkar po las byas pa de d+ha kA dkyil 'khor cho ga bzhin byas la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug ras kyi sku gzugs la/ a ka ru'i bdug pas 'dul bar bya/ dpal
107'a2(rgyud): lha mo la tsan dan dkar po'i bdug pa dbul bar byas zhing gnyi ka la mchod pa dang snyen bkur bya/ rdor ma dkar mo dang / dri chab dbul bar bya// mchod yon sna tshogs dbul bar bya ste/ rigs sngags
107'a3(rgyud): 'chang rtsang mas dus gsum du khrus bya zhing / gos rtsang ma bgos pas mngon du phyogs te// dkyil mo dkrung du 'dug nas/ don yod pa'i zhags pa'i phyag rgya lan bdun byas la/ ji snyed pa'i dri dang phreng
107'a4(rgyud): ba dang / me tog la don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po lan brgya rtsa brgyad da bzlas te// dpal lha mo chen mo'i matong la btags par bya'o// deme tog gzhan gyis mchod pa bya zhing / tsan dan dkar
107'a5(rgyud): po la lan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i bzlas pa'i bdug spos 'bul bar bya'o// / de nas rigs sngags 'chang gis don yod pa'i snying po lan stong rtsa brgyad bzlas te/ par bya zhing // yungs dkar
107'a6(rgyud): re re la bzlas nas/ dpal lha mo la bsnun par bya ste/ stong rtsa brgyad tshor ba dang / dpal lha mo chen mo 'bar bar 'gyur ro// 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi bral ba nas 'od zer 'gyur
107'a7(rgyud): dkyil 'khor gyi yo byad grang smin pa thams cad gser du snang bar 'gyur ro// dpal lha maM chen mo dgug pa 'gyur ro/ shing / ji snyed mno'i bar du bda' bur mo 'gyur ro// lha'i dpal rjes
107'a8(rgyud): spyod par 'dod na/ nyin re bzhin 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug dang / dpal lha mo chen po dus mchod par bya zhing / yod yon gyi snod kyang gzhag par byanapa dkon mchog gsu
107'b1(rgyud): la mchod par bya/ sbyin par ba longs spyod par bya/ bsod nams kyang bya zhing / bal lha mo chen mo tus gsum du mchod par bya/ dpal lha mo rang gi gzugs kyis kyis gnas par 'dod pas/ don yod
107'b2(rgyud): pa'i rgyal po'i khro'i bre'i snying po stong rtsa brgyad bzlas par bya zhing / tsan dan gyi ri lu sdong rtsa brgyad kyis 'dug par bya/ yungs dkar gyis stong rtsa brgyad kyis bsnun par bya ste/ dpal lha me chen mo
107'b3(rgyud): brgyan pa thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ lha'i nor bu dor gsor dang mu tig gis brgyan pa/ lus snang gsal zhol padam kha phyi ba lta bu/ spyan ud pa la ston po lte bur gsal la bad pa snams pa/ 
107'b4(rgyud): ga dan pad ma nor bu dang / rin po chen dang / gser dang / pad ma'ichar 'bebs pa/ rin po che 'bar ba'i bum pa ston phrin/ te/ theg pa/ lha'i bu mo dang / gnod sbyin gyi bu mo brgya stong
107'b5(rgyud): mang po thams cad kyis brgyan pas// lus la zhing 'bar zhing 'dzes pa mang mes yongs su bskor nas 'dun na 'khong bar 'gyur te/ rigs sngags 'bang gis 'jigs par mi bya zhing / sems
107'b6(rgyud): can dga' bar byas la/ gsang sngags 'di lan bdun bzlas par byasa'o// na mo rad na tra ya yA/ na mo ar+ya lo gau ti sha ra ya/ bong de sad dA yA/ ma hA kA ru ni ka yA/ mahA a mo ga pha ra dA yA/ 
107'b7(rgyud): d+yad yA thA ka AM pad ma ni/ pad ma ni tra/ pad mar ge/ pad ma da ri/ pad ma pa ti/ pad ma sne ye/ pad ma pra b+he/ pad ma gI'u re/ pad ma sa na pra ti sh+tsi te/ a ba le gau taM/ sri ye ba ra te ba ra de li/ 
107'b8(rgyud): ni pra sr-i ti pra sid ya/ ku ru ku ru/ ar+ya ba lo ki/ sar+ya lo gi ti bar te/ tu ru tra ru/ bar gi ni/ sa la la/ pad ma bi su sho ti/ pang ma sri ye/ bi tsi te/ bi ma na dare/ ba ra ba ra/ sbar
108'a1(rgyud): 5// ra sa ma yA/ ar+ya pa lo ki ti sha ra yAH/ a me sad t+ya/ a ti shA na/ de bi a mo ban/ ba ra de hUM/ na mo stu te swA hA/ 9lan bdun bzlas pa tsam gyis/ lha mo dpal chen po
108'a2(rgyud): mos phyag rkyang ste// nga rigs sngags 'chang kyi sprin por 'jog par 'gyur zhing / 'di skad ces kyang gsung bar 'gyur ro/ rigs kyi bu tshur shog/ thugs la sra bskyed pa'i gsung las skyes pa/ 
108'a3(rgyud): khyod kyis don yod par zhags pa'i snying po khro bo dang bcas pa grub kyis/ 2lnga don yod pa'i zhags pa'i pad pa ma dri ma mod pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i nga gzungs la zhugs shig/ rang gyi gnas la rang gi/ 
108'a4(rgyud): khyim bzhin du las su bya ba thams cad byos shig/ de nas rigs sngags 'chang gyis yang rigs sngags dang gsang sngags 'di lan gsum bzlas brjod bya'o// na mo rad na tra yA A~M na ma u
108'a5(rgyud): ba lo ki ti shwa ra yA/ bod ti sad ti yA/ ma hA sad dA yA// ma hA ka ru ni ka yA/ oM ba gi ba ti/ ma hA dza de tra/ ba ra ba ra a ba lo ki ti ther te/ kI ri ni sra pa du/ um pa a ma pra/ pi pu
108'a6(rgyud): la ki dI ka re pra par pu tse/ a mo mo ki sra sha ha ste ha sa te/ de'i bag tu dpal le chen mo'i nub ma gnyis las 'o ma'i rgyun 'byung bar 'gyur ro// 'o ma'i rgyun de'i thungs pa tsam gyi mong la/ lha'i me tog pad
108'a7(rgyud): ma dang / ku mu ta lngar mdzes pa'i lha'i lus su gyur/ skye cung zad 'khyil zhing 'khril mig ud pa la sdong po lta bu dang / tshig gsal zhing mi 'am ci'i sgra dbyangs dang ldan par 'gyur ro// don yod
108'a8(rgyud): ba'i rgya mtsho nor bu chen po'i pad ma la rnam par lta ba'i dpal dri mi med pa zhes bya ba'i cho ga zhib me'i rgyal po mngon sum du 'gyur/ cho gzhis mo mang po 'grub par 'gyur/ che le stong phrag brgya thur
108'b1(rgyud): par 'gyur/ rgyal ba 'od dpag med byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs dang thams gcig tu me gzhal med/ kha mchog na chos ston pa mthong bar 'gyur/ rdzu 'phrul gyis nam mkha' la 'gro bar 'gyur/ 
108'b2(rgyud): nor bu chen po pad ma lta ba zhes bya ba'i don yod pa' zhags pa chen po'i 'khor la sgyur bar 'gyur/ rigs sngags 'chang thams cad kyi 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i gtso bo gcig par 'gyur/ 'phags pa
108'b3(rgyud): baspyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi sras su 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sras gcig pur 'gyur/ lnga dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang drin dang lda ma yin dang/ nam mkha' lding dang / 
108'b4(rgyud): 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po rnams kyi bu'i gtso bo gcig pur 'gyur/ rgyal po chen po bzhi'i bu gcig par 'gyur// thams cad du stehA dang pha rol gnon pa dang // brtson 'grus thogs pa med
108'b5(rgyud): ba dang ldan par 'gyuraro// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya dang dkyil 'khor rim par phye ba/ rigs sngags kyi rgyal po gsang sngan pa'i gzungs kyi rgyal po cho gzhib me zab mo dag mngon
108'b6(rgyud): suM du 'gyur lha thams cad kyi gan dang klu thams cad kyi gnas dang mi 'am ci thams cad kyi gnas dang / phug dang khrus kyi gnas thams cad sgo 'bye bar 'gyur ro// gnod sbyin dang srin po'i gnas thes
108'b7(rgyud): sgo'i'abye bar 'gyur ro// zas cad dbang du 'gyur zhing / bgyi ba ci mchis zhes bya ba byed cing 'dug par 'gyur// 'jig rten thams cad kyi ston pa bla ma ci bu 'jig rten mgon po 'dra ba mchod pa'i gnas su/ 
108'b8(rgyud): 'gyur/ 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das po'i gsang sngags dang dkyil 'khor thams cad grub pa chen por 'gyur/ dpal chen po 'khor dang // bcas pa la sbe sregs bgyis na// gsang sngahA
109'a1(rgyud): 'chang de la bu bzhin byams pas/ rang nyid bsnyen bkur yongs su dpyad pa yongs su spyod do// 'dod pa thams cad dang yid du 'ong ba thams cad kyi dgos pa byed par 'gyur te nor bu/ 
109'a2(rgyud): dang 'bru dang / dbyig dang gser dang nor bu dang / mu tig dang / byaM dur+ya dang / shang ka shi la dang / byi ru dang / sa le sbram dang / gdul dang / lha'i nor bu ni po che'i bar thams cad du sbyin par byed do// yul
109'a3(rgyud): ka shi ka'i gros bzang po mang mo sbyin par byed cing / lha'i na bza' dang / btung ba'i bar dang / bdud rtsi'i ro'i bar du sbyin par byed do// gnas thams cad du song ba na yang rtag tu rgyun bu la byas
109'a4(rgyud): pa'i tshul gyis rtag tu phyi bzhin 'brang zhing 'gro bar 'gyuraro// rigs sngags 'tshang rang gi khyim yang rgyal po'i pho grong lcang lo can ji lta ba bzhin du rigs sngags 'chang gi gnal med
109'a5(rgyud): khang mi chog tu 'gyur/ rnam thos kye me'i gnas na 'a bcig pa bzhin du rgyal bar 'gyur ro// tshangs pa dang khyab dang / dbang phyag chen po dus kun du 'ong bar 'gyu ro// gnor sbyin
109'a6(rgyud): kyi skye ben tshun nga dang sa smra rlu chogasamams ca dang / ni sbyin nan pagasang 'grol khor rnams da / rgyun mi dad par 'asrung ba dang / sgyubs rlung bskyed du
109'a7(rgyud): tshig la dag par rngugs pa'i yang rgyas ga 'i zung sa khyis dbyeg thag khrig ba kyai me na 'drug cu pa'i 'i dus bram med pas ba byud pa
109'b1(rgyud): kyi phung po chen po dang ldan par 'gyur ro// rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo 'am/ dge slong ngam dge slong ma 'am/ dge snyen nam/ dge snyen ma 'am/ gang la la zhig gis lha'i nor bu rin po chen
109'b2(rgyud): po dang / rin po che sna bdun dang / lha'i gser dang / gser gyi me tog dang / dngul gyi me tog dang / lha'i gos dang / lha'i rgyan dang / lha'i dri dang / me tog dang / me tog phreng ba dang / byug pa rnam
109'b3(rgyud): re re zhing 'phang du ri'i rgyal po ri rab tsam gyi phung po byas nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa gang gi'i klung gi bye ma snyed bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag drug bcu rtsa bzhi'i rdul phra rab mo snyed kyi de bzhin
109'b4(rgyud): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs sangs rgyas rnams la de bzhin gshegs pa re re la tshul de lta bu so sor rtog cing de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la nyin re re zhig
109'b5(rgyud): lo gcig gis bar du 'dul bar byed/ mchod pa dang snron bkur byedacing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i re re ni spyan ra sngar dri zhim po dang // ldan pa'i til mAr rgya mtsho tsam gyis pa
109'b6(rgyud): bkang ba'i mar me ltam par byed pa'i bsod nams kyi phung po dang ldan par 'gyur/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chen po yongasu bzung por 'gyur/ gal te don yod pa'i zhags pa'i rgya mtsho'i nor bu chen po
109'b7(rgyud): pad ma la nam pA lnga pa'i dpal dri ma med pa don yod pa'i zhags pa'i snying po 'di klog pa dang / bzlas brjod brgya rtsa brgyad byed pa 'di ni bsod nams kyi phung po de lta bu dang ldan par 'gyur zhing / 
109'b8(rgyud): dge ba'i rtsa ba chen po dang ldan par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis bzlas par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis yongs su bzung bar 'gyur// de bzhin
110'a1(rgyud): 1gshegs pa thams cad sku ston par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis lung ston par 'gyur// dpal lha mo chen mo yang mchog thams cad sbyin par 'gyur/ zhing / dus
110'a2(rgyud): kun du de'i khyim tu dpal gnas par 'gyur te/ gang na dpal lha mo chen mo gnas pa der de bzhin gshegs pa gang gang klung gi bye ma snyed bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag drug bcu rtsa bzhi'i rdul phra mo dang
110'a3(rgyud): mnyam pas sa phyogs de nyid tu gnas par 'gyur te/ dpal lha mo de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum yin pa'i phyir/ lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / tshangs pa dang / khyab 'dug
110'a4(rgyud): dang / dbang phyug chen po'i gsang sngags dang cho ga zhib mo dang phyag rgya dang / dkyil 'khor dang / zhi ba dang rgyas pa dang / drag shug spyod pa dang / las sna tshogs gzhan dag pas
110'a5(rgyud): dang dang lha me chen mo'i mchog tu bstan to// dpal lha mo chen po ni thams cad kyi ma yin no// dpal lha mo chen po ni don yod pa'i mchog sbyin pa'o// dpal lha mo ni don yod pa'i zhags pa sbyin pa'o// 
110'a6(rgyud): yod pa'i grags pa rgya chen po sbyin par bya'o// don yod pa'i nam mkha' gzhal med khang sbyin par bya'o// don yod pa'i yon tan sgrags po 'am/ mchog sbyin pa'o// dpal lha mo chen mo nr-i zla dang / nyi mI
110'a7(rgyud): 'od byed pa/ gnas sum bcu rtsa gnyis kyi nang na dpal lha mo chen mo mchog tu ston no// de nas rigs sngags 'chang rtsang mas khrus legs par bya'o// dri chu gsangs shing ba las byung ba'i ltos byug
110'a8(rgyud): pa/ gos rtsang ma bgos pa/ kha zas rtsang ma za ba bya zhing / sha dang chad dang / bag tshong dang / sgog skya dang / ge'u rnams dang / 'dres pa dang / 'bag pa rnams yongs su spang bar bya// 
110'b1(rgyud): kham na pa dang chung bangangan pa dang gos ngan pa dang dris can yongs su spang bar bya/ sems can ngan pa dang / rten ngan pa dang / ngan so can dang / bsod nams rkyen can skye bo ngan pa dang / khrel med pa dang / 
110'b2(rgyud): snying rje med pa dang / byams pa dang / bral ba dang / thub tshong char gyi skye bo rnams spang bar bya'o// gnas ngan pa dang rten ngan pa dang / goms nyem pa dang / mnye'i nas dang / dri ma dran pa yongasu su / 
110'b3(rgyud): bar bya/ gcig gis gcig 'phags pa khabs ngan pa yongasu srang bar byi na / dri dang 'dug spos kyis gsangs te/ mi sba bar 'bras brjod bya/ byams pa dang / snying rje dang dge ba'i sems dang yi
110'b4(rgyud): dge bar gyu dkyis shis rang bar bzhing sring dga' ba dang mgu ba dang / rab tu dga' ba'i sems byas nas/ bzlas brjod pa'o/ 'phags pa sman ras gzigs dbang phyug la
